Current Affairs Commentary

On Honesty and Integrity

People With Aspirations Today Often Attribute the Lack of Solutions in Politics to the Corruption of Officials, and Key Party and National Figures Constantly Strive to Be Honest and Self-Disciplined, and Encourage Their Subordinates With This, Which Can Be Said to Be Repeated Again and Again. However, the Phenomenon of Corruption and Darkness Still Cannot Be Eradicated in Today's Political World. Honesty and Integrity Absolutely Cannot Coexist. In Today's Unequal Society, Absolutely Honest Politics Cannot Be Produced. Even If There Are One or Two Honest Officials Who Want to Build Something Strikingly in This Corrupt Environment, They Will Eventually End Up Assimilating With the Corruption. Tracing Back to Previous History, This Is Invariably True. During the Period of Xianfeng and Tongzhi in the Late Qing Dynasty, Hong Yang Established a Country in Nanjing. Qing Officials Zeng Guofan and Hu Linyi Raised Troops in Hunan and Hubei to Confront the Taiping Army. However, Zeng and Hu Were Both Han Chinese, and the Qing Court Did Not Trust Them. They Specifically Appointed the Banner Man Guan Wen as the Governor-General of Huguang to Supervise Them. Guan Wen's Corruption Was [Blank]. When Hu Was the Governor of Hubei, He Disliked Him Very Much. One Day, He Suddenly Thought of This and Prepared a Memorandum to Impeach Guan's Misconduct and Expose His Acts of Soliciting Power and Accepting Bribes to the Court. He Wandered Around the Room, Unable to Decide. At That Time, Yan Duanmin Public Lived in the Curtain and Asked Strangely. Public Informed Yan That Guan, Although Corrupt, Only Cost Public Hundreds of Thousands of Gold Each Year. However, He Was Stupid and Had No Distant Ambitions. Therefore, He Entrusted All Major Policies to Public Public, and Public Was Able to Calmly Show His Ambitions. If Guan Was Gone, A Smart and Strong Person Would Come, and Everything Would Be Done Personally. Public Would Not Be Able to Do Anything. Hu Realized Greatly. Then He Tried His Best to Befriend Guan Wen. Guan Wen Listened to Hu More and More. Hu Was Able to Become a Famous Minister of the Qing Dynasty Because of Yan's Words. However, the Unremovable Nature of Corrupt Forces Can Also Be Understood.

Before the Qing Dynasty Was Built, Feng Xu Was an Official in Anhui and Held Himself With the Integrity of the Han Dynasty. His Staff Did Not Dare Not to Encourage Each Other to Be Honest. However, Feng Was Involved in the Case of Xu Xilin's Assassination of Governor En. The Relatives of En Who Were Dissatisfied Concocted Rumors Saying That Feng Protected the Revolutionaries. The Qing Court Secretly Sent Prince Zhen to Investigate. Zhen Solicited 100,000 Yuan in Bribes From Feng. As an Honest Official, He Had Never Had Any Ointment From the People in His Pocket to Welcome Him. Before Long, Feng Was Dismissed. This Also Shows That Corruption Is Enough to Corrupt Honest Politics.

The Former Is to Compliment the Corrupt Power and Authority and Survive. The Latter Was Dismissed From Office for Offending the Corrupt Authority. It Is Recorded in History That Every Step Is Incorrect. The Ancients Said, "The Failure of the Country Is Due to the Evil of Officials, and the Loss of Virtue of Officials Is Due to Indulging in Gifts and Regulations." Official Evil and Indulgence in Gifts and Regulations, Corruption Competes With Each Other. It Can Be Said to Be Fierce Today. However, When We Discuss Things, We Should Not Just Hold Ethical and Moral Concepts and Sigh That People's Hearts Are Not Old. The Failure of National Affairs Is Firmly Caused by Corruption, and What Does Corruption Come From? What Does Honesty and Integrity Die From? It Can Not Be Solved by Abstract Nouns Such as Neo-Confucianism's Benevolence, Justice, Faith, and Dao. It Must Be Traced to the Cause of Its Occurrence and the Source of Its Destruction and Govern It Before It Can Be Discussed With the World.

I Have Said It Before. "In Today's Unequal Society, Absolutely Honest Politics Cannot Be Produced." In Society, There Are People Who Get Something Without Work, and There Are People Who Are Diligent All Year Round and Have Nothing. Possession of Everything Is Opposite to Having Nothing. The Privilege Society Is Born. The Power of Officials Is Growing, and the Power of Gentlemen Is Growing. Then the Habits of Pride, Luxury, Licentiousness, and Misconduct and Corruption Arise. Therefore, To Practice Honest Politics Today, We Must First Eradicate This Contradictory Phenomenon and Curb This Unlimited Power of Officials and Gentlemen. On the One Hand, Severe Penalties Are Imposed on Corrupt Officials. The Greater the Official, the Greater the Punishment. Do Not Just Impeach Foxes Without Asking About Wolves. National Affairs Can Be Done. Otherwise, Verbal Bulletins Will Become a Cover, and Honesty and Integrity Will Eventually Be Impossible to Achieve.

Senior Officials Decided

Indefinite Postponement of the Economic Conference

Hull's Proposal to Set a Reopening Date Rejected

Closing Session to Be Held Today

Seven Nations' Representatives to Speak

Australia Finalizes Nine-Nation Silver Agreement Yesterday

(London) The Presidium of the World Economic Conference held a meeting today and decided that the Economic Conference would be indefinitely postponed from Thursday of this week. During the discussion, U.S. Chief Delegate Secretary of State Hull proposed that the sub-committee of the Economic Committee dealing with commercial policy continue its work to discuss the U.S. proposal to extend the tariff truce. Mr. Hull also advocated that the date for the Economic Conference to resume its work should be set before November 1st. Both proposals were rejected due to strong opposition from representatives of other countries. After the adjournment of the Presidium, an announcement was issued stating that the Presidium recommended that the Economic Conference should authorize the Presidium and its Chairman to (1) take all measures that they deem beneficial to the success of the Economic Conference, such as (a) convening any of the sub-committees or panels established by the Economic Conference, or convening representatives of countries that have a special relationship with the issue when discussing a specific issue, (b) referring certain specialized issues to experts for research; (2) set the date for the future convening of the Economic Conference. The plenary session of the Economic Conference is scheduled to be held on Thursday to approve the postponement method. (25th, Havas)

(Wire)

Today's Closing Session

Considering the Report of the Steering Committee

(London) Arrangements have been made in advance for the final plenary session to be held tomorrow. After the reports of the rapporteurs, French Finance Minister Bonnet and British businessman Sir Arthur Salter, are passed, the meeting will consider the report of the Steering Committee and debate the work of the conference and the prospects for the future. There is no doubt that the Steering Committee's proposal to temporarily adjourn the meeting and allow the Steering Committee to consider the matter of reconvening will be approved by the meeting. (26th, Reuters)

(London) A general debate will be held at the plenary session of the Economic Conference tomorrow to discuss various issues that the Presidium has already reviewed, such as the method of convening the next meeting. So far, representatives from seven countries, including the United States, France, Britain, Italy, Germany, the Netherlands, and Czechoslovakia, have signed up to participate in the general debate. (26th, Havas)

(London) The Japanese delegation held a full-power meeting on the 25th and decided that if there is an opportunity at the Economic Conference on the 27th, it will reiterate Japan's views, advocating the unconditional application of the most-favored-nation clause and the elimination of trade barriers. Ishii has already prepared a draft speech. (25th, Japanese League Wire)

Steering Committee Will Not Be Dissolved

(London) It is reported that the final meeting of the World Economic Conference tomorrow will decide on the continuation of the conference, instructing the Steering Committee to reconvene the conference when the environment indicates that discussions can be successful. The Steering Committee's Guidance Committee will continue to serve, and countries can be represented by their ambassadors.

U.S. Prepares to Propose New Monetary Recommendations

(London) It is reported that the Chairman of the Monetary and Financial Committee, American Cox, will propose a form of government bond. This proposal will greatly reform the European standard, so if this proposal is established, it will have a far-reaching impact. (26th, Reuters)

Yan Huiqing Returns to Moscow

(London) Dr. Yan Huiqing has returned to Moscow today. No Chinese representative will speak at tomorrow's plenary session. (26th, Reuters)

Australia Signs Silver Agreement

(London) Australia is scheduled to sign the silver agreement this afternoon. This is the only news about the World Economic Conference today. (26th, Reuters)

Pessimism in Mexican Silver Circles

Mexico City Although the Mexican Minister of Finance also signed the silver agreement of the World Economic Conference, silver market leaders here are pessimistic, believing that the agreement lacks clarity. If the silver price matches the exchange rate of the U.S. dollar, Mexico can benefit, but according to their opinion, artificial inflation of prices raised by agreement methods will definitely not succeed. (25th, Reuters)

Criticism from the President of the U.S. Mining Association

Salt Lake City, USA The President of the American Silver Mining Association, Meng Feili, said here today that plans regarding silver will not be stable unless silver is recognized as a basic currency. The independent actions of the United States have been clearly demonstrated in the silver agreement established in London. It is incredible that U.S. representatives were induced to agree to any plan that does not recognize silver as a primary currency. U.S. representatives went to London with the clear intention of the Senate and House of Representatives to achieve this goal through unremitting efforts. If this is not the case, they will not obtain the consent of Congress. If only a method is established to regard silver as a commodity, even if it is beneficial, it will be insufficient. (25th, Reuters)

The World's Attention is on the Dumping of Japanese Goods

Ishii Appeals Loudly to the Country

Advocates Controlling Exports to Seek Reconciliation

(Tokyo) The Japanese economic representative, Ishii, broadcast a speech to Japan by radio on the 24th. The content is as follows: Before and after the opening of the economic conference, what caught our attention was the profoundness of the economic problems that all countries in the world are worried about and the intensity of competition among countries. It is truly shocking for us that all countries are vigorously promoting that Japan is surpassing other countries and invading the world market. The U.S. President and the British Prime Minister also believe in the figures of this propaganda. Once the World Economic Conference breaks down, it will immediately turn into a world economic war, as people in all countries have said. At the beginning of this economic war, Japan is uniquely regarded as the invading king of the world market, and there is no doubt that Japan will be oppressed in various ways and in various forms. Japan must be prepared in advance, and the most important thing is to implement strict control over overseas exports. (26th, Japanese League Wire)

Japanese Pharmaceutical Industry Competes with Foreign Countries

(Tokyo) The Japanese pharmaceutical industry has made great progress in recent years, with an annual output of 40 to 50 million yuan. However, imported drugs into the country are worth more than 10 million yuan every year. The Ministry of Interior's Health Bureau has decided to actively revitalize domestic production. The specific method is to organize a pharmaceutical export association with famous pharmaceutical companies in Tokyo and Osaka. On the one hand, it prevents the import of foreign goods, and on the other hand, it actively promotes foreign exports. At present, the most promising markets overseas are South America, Southeast Asia, and India. (26th, Japanese League Wire)

Britain, India, and Japan Will

Hold a Meeting in India

Japanese Cotton Industry Agrees to Discuss Low Prices

London British Trade Department Parliamentary Secretary Perkin stated on behalf of the government in the Lower House today that the Japanese cotton industry has agreed to discuss the low prices of competitive products with the British cotton industry under certain restrictions. Britain has proposed that representatives from Britain, India, and Japan hold a three-party discussion in India, covering all textile matters related to the three parties.

The British government hopes that the Japanese government can represent its cotton industry to accept this proposal and obtain a satisfactory agreement through discussion. (25th, Reuters)

(Tokyo) Regarding the issue of the Japan-India Treaty, the expiration date of October 10th is approaching, but the British government and its operators have not shown sincerity. The Indian government is also worried about the attitude of the British government, so it is difficult to expect an effective solution. Therefore, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs believes that it is necessary to change the fundamental policy of commercial diplomacy with India. According to the reports of Ambassador Matsudaira to Britain and Consul General Miyake to Calcutta on the 25th, although Britain and India are unwilling to formally codify commercial negotiations with Japan, they hope that the substantial commercial relations with Japan will continue to be good. Even after the treaty is abolished, Britain and India are still prepared to take measures to avoid drastic changes. On the other hand, Japanese business operators, regarding the impact of the abolition of the treaty, with a deep determination and spirit of unity, delaying the dispatch of representatives is counterproductive. Therefore, they also advised the foreign affairs authorities. After considering the above matters, the authorities have generally decided that the government representative, Minister Sawada, and his party will depart from Tokyo on August 10th and take the Terukuni Maru from Kobe to India on the 11th. (26th, Dentsu Wire)

(Tokyo) According to a telegram from Consul General Miyake stationed in Simla to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the Indian government has issued a consultation letter consisting of fifteen items to various industry groups due to the need to apply the Industrial Protection Law, ordering a reply before the end of the month. If the reply is insufficient, representatives of various industries will be summoned to inquire about the details. The consultation letter includes production status, import ratio, import price, labor status, and comparison with the cost of domestic production. Especially for Japanese goods, detailed investigations are required. Therefore, the Indian government apparently wants to use this to build countermeasures for the Simla meeting, and its intention seems to be to further suppress Japanese goods. (26th, Dentsu Wire)

South Africa Rejects Japanese Goods

Japan's Protest Ineffective

(Tokyo) The Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs believes that South Africa and the Straits Settlements' increase in tariffs on Japanese goods violates the tariff truce case and protested to the British government. Ambassador Matsudaira to Britain reported on the 26th that the British government replied that the colonies' increase in tariffs on Japanese hats, lace, embroidery, etc. was before the establishment of the tariff truce case, so Britain believes that it does not violate the case. (26th, Japanese League News Agency)

U.S. Government Will

Implement the National Recovery Plan Starting Today

Will Do Everything Possible to Shut Foreign Goods Out of the Domestic Market

Various Industries Have Submitted Industry Regulations One After Another

Speculation in the Grain Market Swept Away

(Washington) The troublesome issues in the grain market have been resolved because the national exchanges have negotiated new industry regulations and rectified themselves. The U.S. government will now fully implement its National Recovery Plan starting on Thursday. It is expected that various other industries will also follow the food merchants and quickly comply with government expectations, increase wages, and shorten working hours. In order to reward the cooperation of the industry, the government will also do everything possible to assist various industries, and even prepare to shut foreign goods that compete fiercely with U.S. goods out of the U.S. market. At the same time, the government has started mailing cotton survey orders to cotton planters. The government now plans to provide cash subsidies for destroyed cotton seedlings, giving 20 yuan per acre for land that can produce 100 to 124 pounds of cotton per acre. Up to now, the textile, steel, and petroleum industries have submitted industry regulations. In addition, the government has formulated temporary industry regulations based on the general principles in the textile industry regulations for various industries to temporarily adopt before negotiating industry regulations. It is expected that various industries will accept them on Thursday. (25th, National Wire)

(Washington) The U.S. grain exchanges have been reorganized internally and submitted new industry regulations today. According to this new plan, malpractices such as price surges and squeezes can be completely eliminated. From now on, grain trading will lose most of its speculative color and become a real transaction. The first article is to permanently limit the price fluctuations. The price of wheat cannot fluctuate more than five cents in a day, corn four cents, and other miscellaneous grains three cents. This restriction will prevent the food market from attracting the attention of speculators. Secondly, the bad habit of buying futures at a price different from the market price on the same day is completely abolished. Again, brokers are forced to immediately request additional margin when the market situation changes, and the percentage varies according to the amount of their transaction. For example, the percentage of margin for 100,000 bushels will be greater than 50,000 bushels to prevent speculators from creating a position to manipulate the market. The total amount of long and short positions that each merchant can make will also be regulated, that is, the operation of grain purchase capital groups will also have considerable restrictions. It is reported that Agricultural Recovery Administrator Peek approved these industry regulations and will promote them in exchanges across the country. In addition, grain traders also submitted a part of the proposed industry regulations today after being ordered by the government to improve trade methods. A formal industry regulation will be submitted soon. Tonight, it is heard that grain experts agree with this plan and believe that this move will have an important international impact, which can avoid the dumping of foreign grain, and the permitted price fluctuation limit is still sufficient to guarantee that there can be an active market at any time. (25th, National Wire)

(Washington) Economic Recovery Bureau Director General Johnson declared that more than 10,000 employers have issued declarations one after another, expressing their participation in President Roosevelt's National Economic Recovery Plan. Therefore, telegrams and telephones were temporarily crowded. In addition, General Johnson asked employers to pay attention not to engage in speculative price increases before purchasing power increases. (26th, Havas)

(Washington) General Johnson, the implementation personnel of the Industrial Recovery Act, said that according to the replies obtained from various parties based on President Roosevelt's proposal, it is expected that five to six million people will be able to obtain new jobs around September 1. (26th, Reuters)

San Francisco Tonight, the governors listened quietly in the state governors' meeting here to President Roosevelt's speech broadcast on the radio in Washington, asking the states to cooperate with the central government to consolidate the position of various public debts, and instructed the governors to gather in Washington in mid-winter to discuss public debt issues. (25th, National Wire)

Anecdotes of Roosevelt

Always Purse His Lips and Whistle When Annoyed

Reuters New York, Syracuse U.S. Treasury Secretary Woodin, who is a composer in his spare time, recently discovered that President Roosevelt always purses his lips and whistles when annoyed. Germany Implements Eugenics

Eliminating Those Unfit to Survive

Reuters, Berlin, 26th - The German cabinet will soon approve a law to eliminate those unfit to survive. This law stipulates that any person who is an incurable drunkard, sex offender, epileptic, or suffers from an incurable disease that is likely to be passed on to future generations, may be forcibly eliminated if a majority of specialist doctors determine that it is necessary for the happiness of the country. However, they are allowed to appeal to a specially established higher health court in the future.

(National Daily, Berlin, 25th) The German government today promulgated a new decree that anyone suffering from neurasthenia, epilepsy, or significant hereditary physiological defects shall not be allowed to have children. The government's opinion on this measure is that healthy parents generally produce only one or two children, while parents with unhealthy bodies and minds also produce countless children with the same unhealthy bodies and minds. These unhealthy children must ultimately be raised by the state, and the state treasury spends hundreds of millions of dollars each year, which is taken from healthy parents who produce healthy children. Therefore, in the current situation, there is no other good way to provide relief except to vigorously eliminate their reproductive capacity. Therefore, the government believes that this new decree is a charitable decree and will surely benefit from it in the future. Furthermore, in order to prevent people from recognizing this decree as a punishment for people who are physically or mentally weak, criminals are not included in the category of eliminating reproduction, and separate provisions will be made for the disposal of criminal reproduction. This new decree will be implemented from January 1st next year.

Drafted by the Ministry of Justice

Measures for Solving Sexual Desire of Prisoners

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Justice has drafted measures for prisoners to solve their sexual desires. The content and nature are different from those in the former Qing Dynasty. In the past, it was a matter of succession. For example, if a newly married man, who is the only son, suddenly commits a serious crime or is sentenced to life imprisonment or many years of imprisonment, the family requests that his wife be allowed to cohabitate with him so that she can become pregnant and avoid extinction. After obtaining permission from the court, they are temporarily released for cohabitation for a set period of one or two days and then return to prison. This time, the planned measures are not for the issue of succession, but to take reward measures. For example, if they behave well in prison until the statutory period, they can have the hope of resolving their sexual desires. If they are divided into several levels and reach a certain level and their good behavior meets the conditions, they will have this right. Otherwise, they will have no such hope. This is to influence young people to get on the right track. Because there is this hope, they will definitely behave well in prison, and their bad behavior and character can therefore be expected to be quickly changed. This measure will be decided after it is reviewed by the central government. (Special dispatch, 26th)

Hungarian Prime Minister Discusses with Mussolini

Revising the Treaty of Trianon

At the Same Time, Dealing with Hitler's Policy on the Danube

Methods to Ease the Ethnic Disputes between the United States and Canada Will Also Be Discussed

Reuters, Rome, 26th - Hungarian Prime Minister Dr. Gömbös and Foreign Minister Dr. Kánya arrived here last night. It is expected that the main purpose of their visit is to conduct international talks. The possibility of revising the Treaty of Trianon will probably be discussed with Italian Prime Minister Mussolini and others today. In addition, methods to ease the ethnic disputes between the United States and Canada and solutions to the difficulties caused by German Chancellor Hitler's vigorous implementation of his economic and political policies in the Danube countries may also be discussed. The Treaty of Trianon was signed by the Allied Powers and Hungary on June 4, 1920. According to this treaty, Hungary lost a lot of land. Its northern part was ceded to Czechoslovakia, and its southern part was ceded to Yugoslavia. At the same time, it gave up Hungary and other lands formerly belonging to the Austro-Hungarian Empire. Hungary's independence may not be transferred without the consent of the League of Nations. Havas, Rome, 25th - Hungarian Prime Minister Gömbös, accompanied by Foreign Minister Kanya and his entourage, departed from the Hungarian capital last night and will arrive here tonight. The talks between the Italian and Hungarian authorities will continue for two days. At present, a large-scale movement is underway internationally to prepare for the transformation of Central and Eastern Europe and to establish a foundation for peace. The arrival of the Hungarian political leader in Italy coincides with this movement. Italy is extremely concerned about maintaining the balance of power in Central and Eastern Europe and will definitely use its potential power in Central and Eastern Europe in a fair and honest manner to achieve a stable balance. It is deliberately the case that during the talks between the Italian and Hungarian authorities, Mussolini will probably not firmly support all events that could lead Hungary and its neighbors to extremes, such as the issue of revising the treaty that Hungarian newspapers have repeatedly demanded. Hungarian people here refuted the remarks of the Hungarian newspaper Az Est, saying that Gömbös's visit to Italy will definitely not realize the Eastern Locarno Treaty and revise the treaty.

Havas, Rome, 26th - Italian Prime Minister Mussolini met with Hungarian Prime Minister Gömbös and Foreign Minister Kanya for a long time. This afternoon, the Italian Prime Minister will go to the residence of the Hungarian delegation to return the visit to Gömbös. In addition, economic talks will be held by experts from both sides. The true meaning of the Italian Prime Minister's talks with the Hungarian Prime Minister is still difficult to determine, but political circles believe that the main point of the two people's talks should be the issue of the relations between Hungary and Austria. Italy hopes that the economic proximity between Hungary and Austria will increase Italy's status for Germany and the Little Entente countries. Regarding the Italian Prime Minister's talks with the Hungarian Prime Minister, Italian newspapers have repeatedly said that since the establishment of the Four-Power Pact, all issues have begun to be discussed, which is completely different from the situation when Prime Minister Gömbös visited Italy in November. The Envoy newspaper said, "The Four-Power Pact has fundamentally changed the international political atmosphere, and all proposals for international rapprochement or understanding are possible because of this pact." The People's Daily hopes that the Italian Prime Minister and the Hungarian Prime Minister will start discussing "issues of common interest to the two countries, because this issue has special value in the new international situation created by the Four-Power Pact."

Insufficient Protection of Citizens

Air Defense Exercise Discovers Danger

China United News Agency, Tokyo, 26th - Regarding the air defense exercise in Tokyo, after the results of the two preliminary exercises, the military has conducted a rigorous scientific study and found that Tokyo has many shortcomings. Without improvement, it may not be enough to defend against enemy air raids. The so-called shortcomings in air defense are as follows: (1) The subway is the best refuge for citizens, but the subway in Tokyo is only five to ten feet deep from the ground. Bombs with a yield of ten to twenty-five killoton are sufficient to destroy this equipment and can only accommodate 130,000 people. (2) The cement and steel bars used in various high-rise buildings are very thin. Bombing with a 500-kiloton bomb is sufficient to penetrate five floors, and the equipment in each house is very small. (3) The iron pipes for tap water and fire are buried very shallow underground. Once bombed in the air, it cannot be guaranteed to be safe and sound. It must be remedied as soon as possible. Once something happens, it cannot guarantee the water and fire needed by citizens. Only after two small exercises have such major shortcomings been discovered, then the air defense problem in Tokyo after the big exercise may become a major problem.

Observe the Situation and Await

Lushan Conference Resolution

Feng's Attitude Remains Firm

Personnel Adjustments in the Chahar Military

Special dispatch from Beiping: The solution to the Chahar situation has still not been found. Recently, Feng expressed again that unless the central government has an entire anti-Japanese plan, the name of the Anti-Japanese Allied Army cannot be cancelled. Generals such as Fang Zhenwu have also issued a telegram stating that unless the truce agreement is overturned and the lost territory is recovered, the anti-Japanese goal will not be achieved, and military action cannot be ended. The Pingfang authorities believe that these statements by Feng and others are absolutely non-negotiable. Therefore, since Deng Zhexi, Li Xin, and others left Ping for Tianjin, and Ma Boyuan returned to Ping from Zhangjiakou to report on his mission, the mediation action has completely stalled. Song Zheyuan asked for leave to recuperate due to a recurrence of his back pain and planned to live temporarily in the Western Hills. Therefore, the future of the Chahar situation is becoming more pessimistic. However, Pingfang is still waiting for the Lushan Conference to indicate the final decision.

The troops that entered Chahar to fill the defenses were originally Pang Bingxun's 40th Army, Guan Linzheng's 25th Division, and the troops of He Sui and Feng Qinzai. Pang's troops were the main force, so Pang was appointed as the commander-in-chief, and all armies were under Pang's control. Since the mobilization, Pang's troops have been in the front, followed by He's and Guan's troops, gradually departing from Juyong Pass, advancing along the railway line from Kangzhuang to Huailai, then to Shacheng, and then to Xiahuayuan, with great momentum. However, Pang's troops were mostly reorganized from the old Northwest Army. Since arriving near Xiahuayuan and Xinzhuangzi and approaching Feng's troops, a part suddenly acted freely. Pang changed the brigade commander of that part and urgently sought to reorganize it. The day before yesterday, near Xiahuayuan, another part was unstable, and troops were immediately sent to suppress it. There was a slight movement near the railway, and the situation was tense for a while and then calmed down. After this incident, in order to rectify military discipline and consolidate defense, the current defense area was slightly adjusted. Since the day before yesterday, Pang's troops have withdrawn from the front, and Wang Jingjiu's division has been transferred to fill the defense. Wang's troops have departed from Baoding and are heading out of Juyong Pass. Wang himself also came to Ping from Baoding at 1:00 p.m. today to visit He Yingqin and ask for instructions. Pang Bingxun also sent Deputy Commander Ma Dewu to Ping to visit the authorities due to the change of defense area and to contact various parties. He also returned to the defense area today to report on his mission. At present, the final line of the troops in the front has reached near Xinzhuangzi. The troops of Sun Liangcheng and Fang Zhenwu of Feng's troops are between Xinzhuangzi and Xuanhua, only fourteen or five li apart, forming a confrontation. However, all troops have been ordered to temporarily remain in their original defenses and await orders. Although the situation is tense, there is no change temporarily. Sun Dianying's troops are departing one after another. A part has arrived in Baotou, and the majority are still concentrated between Chaigoubao and Zhangjiakou and Xuanhua, waiting for money to move west. Sun Dianying suddenly fell ill and was hospitalized in Suiyuan the day before yesterday and telegraphed Pingfang, requesting famous doctors to go for diagnosis and treatment. The date of going to Baotou must be slightly delayed. The entire movement of the troops has also been affected. It is difficult to predict when they will be completely evacuated from Chahar. (Reached on July 25)

Worldwide Market Rejects Japanese Goods

Countries Lay a Net of Vigilance Against Japan

Tokyo Houchi Shimbun reported on the 23rd that, due to Japan's industrial rationalization and low labor costs, all of its goods are poised to sweep the global market. Recently, the exchange rate has fallen, further accelerating this trend. As a result, various countries around the world have jointly laid a net of vigilance against it. Since the failure of the World Economic Conference, economic nationalism has intensified. Japanese goods have been transformed and are now being rejected by markets worldwide. There have been frequent reports of suspending most-favored-nation treatment and abrogating trade agreements. Currently, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs is continuously receiving reports from various locations about the increasingly deteriorating anti-Japanese sentiment. After Japan withdrew from the League of Nations, it has strived to plan individual reciprocal agreements from an independent diplomatic standpoint to break through the difficult economic situation. However, circumstances have presented various difficulties. According to a survey by the authorities, the situation of worldwide market rejection of Japanese goods is as follows:

(1) Britain: It has raised tariffs on Japanese goods such as iron products, rubber products, porcelain, silk and silk fabrics, dyes, and hats to counteract them and advocates the abolition of the Anglo-Japanese Treaty of Commerce. (2) British India: It has raised tariffs on rayon fabrics, cotton fabrics, towels, cotton yarn, paper, cement, iron products, glass, rubber, shoes, leather, pencils, umbrellas, beer, soap, raw silk, shell buttons, porcelain, cotton cloth, etc. The Sino-Indian Treaty of Commerce completely expires on October 10th. (3) Australia: It is currently investigating the types of Japanese goods being dumped and is consulting with the British government on ways to reject them. (4) Federated Malay States: It recently raised tariffs on Japanese goods such as cotton cloth and rayon. (5) Johor, Southern Malaya: It has also raised tariffs on Japanese goods. (6) British East Africa: In addition to the previously set ad valorem tax on Japanese goods such as rayon cloth, cotton fabrics, bicycles, and wool blankets, it has also imposed specific duties and prevented the import of cheap goods. (7) British West Africa: The British government has announced the abolition of the Anglo-Japanese Treaty of Commerce. (8) South African Federation: Although it has not yet outwardly rejected Japanese goods, it is likely to follow the trend in other British territories, given the situation in those regions. (9) Malta: It has prevented the import of cheap Japanese goods such as cotton products and groceries. (10) Dutch East Indies: It recently announced restrictions on the import of Japanese cement and raised tariffs on cotton cloth, beer, etc. (11) The United States: In 1931 and 1932, Congress passed bills imposing countervailing duties and other special taxes on imported Japanese goods. Currently, it has specifically raised tariffs on Japanese goods. On the one hand, it restricts the import of cheap Japanese goods through administrative orders in accordance with the National Industrial Recovery Act. (12) Egypt: It has raised special taxes on Japanese cotton yarn cloth and rayon fabrics. (13) Turkey: It has stipulated import quotas and prevented the import of cheap Japanese goods. (14) Greece: Since June 23, it has prohibited the exchange of cheap goods for Japanese imports. Hereafter, it will not allow Japanese goods to be imported into Greece except through barter. (15) Belgium: It is currently discussing restricting the import of Japanese goods and studying ways to reject them.

The War Zone Has Already Been Taken Over

The Puppet Army Has Started to Be Reorganized into the Second Contingent

The Beining Railway Will Be Open to Traffic After the Takeover is Completed

Whether Our Sovereignty is Restricted is Still Questionable

A special dispatch from Peiping: The issue of the puppet army, which posed the greatest obstacle to the takeover of the war zone, has been completely resolved after days of consultation. The large sum of money demanded by the puppet army has been successively remitted to Tangshan by the takeover committee. The first payment was 140,000 yuan, and the second was over 100,000 yuan, with more to follow. The puppet army, having achieved its wish, complied and began to concentrate in Tangshan, Xugezhuang, Beidaihe, Luohe, Fengrun, and other places from the previous day, awaiting reorganization. The puppet army in the Ninghe area completely withdrew to Fengrun yesterday, and other scattered puppet troops are also concentrating in designated locations nearby and will begin reorganization immediately. The scope of the reorganization remains as originally agreed, with 10,000 men, 4,000 to be reorganized and 6,000 to be demobilized. The demobilized soldiers will be transported to Machang and sent back to their hometowns separately. The first train will be loaded with goods in Anshan and depart for Xikai tomorrow (the 26th), and the second and third trains will be loaded with goods in Luanxian the day after tomorrow (the 27th). The fourth train will be loaded with goods in Xugezhuang on the 28th. Li Jichun requested six months to complete the reorganization, but after negotiation, it was limited to three months. The 4,000 reorganized puppet soldiers will be formed into the Second Special Police Contingent, stationed in Luanzhou and Fengrun counties. Shi Yousan's troops are currently being negotiated with by Liu Shisun of the takeover committee, and they are generally ready and are being successively transferred to Yutian County to await reorganization. In the future, they will be incorporated into the Second Contingent, merging with the 4,000 reorganized puppet soldiers. The Hebei Provincial Government will separately organize 4,000 special police officers to form the First Contingent, which will be directly trained by the provincial government and stationed in various counties in the war zone. The Committee for Taking Over the War Zone is proceeding with the takeover. In addition to dispatching teams along two routes as originally planned, Li Zeyi will be stationed in Peiping to facilitate contact during the takeover and handle negotiations with all parties. Yin Tong and Wei Jian will be in Tianjin to handle all matters, and Lei Shourong and Xue Zhiheng will be stationed in Tangshan to facilitate contact at any time. Tao Shangming will be responsible for the takeover in northern Peiping. When taking over counties with Japanese troops stationed, the Japanese military will send personnel to accompany the takeover team. Within the scope of the puppet army's territory, Li Jichun will send personnel to accompany the takeover team. Yu Xuezhong, Chairman of the Takeover Committee, will oversee everything. Yu had originally received a telegram summoning him to the Lushan Conference, but he was unable to attend because he was in the process of taking over the war zone. The takeover on the eastern route will begin in Tangshan. Song Naigan, the Tangshan Special Public Security Bureau Chief dispatched by the provincial government, arrived in Tangshan with Lei Shourong the day before yesterday (the 23rd). The takeover was originally scheduled for yesterday (the 24th), but it could not be carried out as scheduled because it was necessary to consult with Guo Xixian, the puppet bureau chief appointed by Li Jichun, on the handover procedures. Li Jichun hosted a banquet yesterday to welcome them and introduce Song and Guo to discuss the matter, and it was decided to carry out the takeover today. At 10 a.m. today (the 25th), Song led the police to the bureau, and Guo handled the handover. As a result, Tangshan returned to its former appearance. The county magistrates and public security bureau chiefs of the counties on the eastern route also departed from Tianjin today. After the county magistrates and public security bureau chiefs arrive in Tangshan, they will take over the respective counties and bring police to maintain local order. On the northern front of Peiping, Tao Shangming and others first went to Miyun to contact Suzuki, the Japanese brigade commander, and then began the takeover. This morning at 4 a.m., Tao, along with Xu Wenquan, the county magistrate of Huairou, Sun Shutang, the county magistrate of Miyun, and Sun Weishan, the county magistrate of Ji County, and 20 security police officers, departed from Jiaodaokou inside Andingmen in a long-distance bus. Because of heavy rain in northern Peiping the night before, the roads were muddy and the bus was moving very slowly. It only passed the Qiaotou Village bus station in Huairou County at 11 a.m. The 40-mile section from Huairou to Miyun was flooded along the road, making driving even more difficult. It was not until around 2 p.m. that they reached Miyun. It was originally planned to return to Peiping this afternoon and take over Miyun and Huairou counties tomorrow, but because it was too late, they were unable to return. They should be able to return to Peiping tomorrow. According to Li Zeyi, most of the Japanese 8th Division in the Miyun area has withdrawn to the Great Wall, with only two companies remaining in Miyun. After our takeover, the Japanese troops there are expected to withdraw completely.

Negotiations for the opening of the Beining Railway are currently being handled by Qian Zongze. It was originally prepared to resume operations as soon as possible, but the Japanese and puppet army sides created additional complications, and it could not be realized. It has now been decided to wait until the takeover of the war zone is completed before seeking to open the railway. As for the postal service in eastern Luan, it has been fully restored. Telegrams in Qinhuangdao, Tangshan, Beidaihe, and other places have also been sent and received as usual.

The members of the negotiation team this time are purely Japanese, and some of them are not from the military or political circles but are compradores. Therefore, the consultations in Dalian, Tangshan, and other places are generally considered to be quite like brokerage deals and not genuine negotiations. The appointed county magistrates and public security bureau chiefs in the war zone are mostly those who can speak Japanese in order to facilitate contact with the Japanese side, and some have obtained informal consent from the other party beforehand. The war zone is essentially a buffer zone, and it remains questionable whether our side will be subject to considerable restrictions in terms of sovereignty and administration after the takeover. (July 25)

Serious Famine in Northern Fujian

Early Rice Crop Fails and People are Dying of Hunger

Various Organizations Have Taken Measures to Provide Relief

A dispatch from Fuzhou: Yong'an, Shaxian, Mingxi, and Qingliu counties in northern Fujian, as well as Gutian, Yongtai, Minqing, and Minhou counties near the province, have all suffered from banditry and warfare in recent years, leading to the flight of farmers, the abandonment of farmland, and a sharp reduction in rice production. In addition, this year's spring was marked by severe drought, and the early summer brought heavy rains and disasters, resulting in the failure of the early rice crop. Although rice merchants from the provincial capital have purchased and transported sea rice to provide relief, the price is high, costing more than 18 yuan per dan. Moreover, it is only sold in county towns, and poor people in the countryside can only dig up grass roots and tree bark to fill their stomachs, with people dying of hunger everywhere, a truly unbearable sight. Take the western countryside of Min County, the seat of the provincial capital, as an example. According to the survey reports of the 8th and 12th District Offices, more than 2,000 farmers in Nanting, Xuefeng, Daping, Zhuyuan, Qiangtou, Changji, Junxi, Huangpu, Luoyang, and Chayang townships are unable to cultivate and have nothing to eat. More than ten people die every day. Given that the situation is so severe in areas adjacent to the provincial capital, one can only imagine the cruel conditions in the remote counties upstream. Therefore, the Provincial Government's Department of Civil Affairs and Relief Committee have been receiving urgent telegrams from various counties calling for help every day. There are still two months until the autumn harvest (in fact, the late rice harvest is also not very large). Without urgent relief measures, all the starving people will die of hunger. Moreover, after Peng Dehuai and Luo Binghui of the Jiangxi Communists led large groups of bandits into the Fujian border and ravaged the area, even well-off families have been bankrupted. Currently, no fewer than several thousand refugees from Jianning, Taining, Mingxi, and Qingliu counties have fled to Shunchang, Jiangle, Jian'ou, and Nanping. Due to the hot weather and lack of food, many people die every day. Several dozen representatives were specially sent to the province the day before yesterday to petition for relief funds and to establish shelters, a truly tragic situation. The Provincial Relief Committee plans to borrow funds from the banking sector and send personnel to Shanghai to purchase rice and transport it back for price stabilization. At the same time, it will request substantial funds from the central government for relief. The Provincial Government Committee also resolved yesterday to raise relief funds, organize a fundraising team, with the Chairman of the Provincial Government as the team leader, and invite Minnan leaders in various Nanyang ports and the presidents of hometown associations in various provinces to serve as team leaders and jointly raise funds for relief. The above two matters, price stabilization and relief distribution, are both in the planning stage, but have not yet been implemented. Therefore, it is difficult to predict when they can be realized. As for the relief measures in the western countryside of the provincial capital, the County Chamber of Commerce, County Government, Red Cross Society, Wanzihui, Weishan Society, Shushan Society, and other organizations have jointly established an office to assist starving people with food and are expected to raise 3,000 yuan within five days to purchase rice for distribution. (July 21)

Hunan Province Issues

Construction Bonds of 10 Million Yuan

6 Million Yuan to Build the Hongbao Light Railway

3 Million Yuan to Repay Old Debts to Bank of Communications

A dispatch from Changsha: Hunan Province has now decided to convert the Hongbao Highway (from Hongjiang to Baoqing) into a light railway, which is expected to require approximately 6 million yuan. However, Hunan Province's public and private finances are in dire straits and truly unable to afford this. It has invited Tang Youren, Zhang Gongquan, and others to Hunan to inspect the road administration and welcome the Shanghai banking sector to invest in Hunan. At that time, Zhang Gongquan and others stated that the Hunan provincial governments had accumulated debts of more than 3 million yuan in loans from the Bank of Communications and the Bank of China, plus more than 5 million yuan in interest, and that the old debts must be paid off first before investment would be permitted. After repeated consultations between He Jian and Zhang Gongquan and others, it was decided that (1) the old debts of the Bank of Communications and the Bank of China would be allowed to be repaid with reduced interest, and (2) the Hunan Provincial Government would issue construction bonds of 10 million yuan, with approximately 3 million yuan used to repay the principal of the old debts of the Bank of Communications and the Bank of China, and the remaining 6 million yuan would be used by Zhang Gongquan and others to introduce Shanghai banks to mortgage cash as funds for the construction of the Hongbao Light Railway. Before the railway is fully completed, the deed tax and business tax revenue will be used to repay the principal and interest on a regular basis. After the railway is completed, the operating income of the railway will be used to repay the principal and interest. The "Regulations on Hunan Provincial Construction Bonds" have been drafted by the Hunan Finance and Construction Departments, submitted to He Jian for approval, and forwarded to the central government for review and promulgation. Zhang Zhongjun, the representative of the Fourth Route General Headquarters stationed in Nanjing, telegraphed that the Central Political Committee had already approved this proposal in principle. At the same time, Tang Youren's Secretary-General telegraphed that the prospects were smooth and that it could be submitted to the next Central Political Committee for resolution. The regulations are as follows:

Article 1: The Hunan Provincial Government issues construction bonds of 10 million yuan, named Hunan Provincial Construction Bonds, to repay old bank debts, establish financial credibility, and raise funds to build the Bao Hong Light Railway.

Article 2: The interest rate of these bonds is set at 6% per annum.

Article 3: These bonds are issued at 98% of their face value.

Article 4: These bonds are issued on July 1, 1933.

Article 5: Interest on these bonds is paid twice a year, on June 30 and December 31.

Article 6: These bonds will be redeemed in ten years by lottery from June 30, 1933, until December 31, 1943, until the principal and interest are fully repaid. The lottery shall be held twice a year, on June 15 and December 15, and payment shall begin at the end of the same month. The Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Audit shall send personnel to supervise each lottery.

Article 7: The number of bonds to be drawn in each lottery and the amount of principal to be redeemed shall be in accordance with the attached table.

Article 8: Funds for the principal and interest of these bonds shall be allocated from the Hunan Provincial deed tax and business tax revenue on a regular basis in accordance with the numbers listed in the principal and interest repayment table. If it is insufficient, it shall be permitted to allocate funds from other revenue to make up the difference.

Article 9: The principal and interest funds of these bonds shall be specially deposited in the Bank of China, the Bank of Communications in Shanghai, and the Hunan Provincial Bank, and shall be managed by the Fund Management Committee. The Fund Management Committee shall be composed of one person each from the provincial government and the auditing agency, as well as representatives from the Bankers' Association, the Money Industry Association, and the Chamber of Commerce. Its management rules shall be stipulated separately.

Article 10: The bonds are divided into three denominations: 1,000 yuan, 100 yuan, and 10 yuan, all of which are unregistered.

Article 11: The Bank of China, the Bank of Communications, and the Hunan Provincial Bank shall be the managing agencies for redeeming the principal and paying the interest of these bonds.

Article 12: The bonds drawn in the lottery and the matured interest coupons may be used to pay all taxes in the province.

Article 13: These bonds may be freely bought, sold, and mortgaged. When it is necessary to pay a deposit for official duties in the province, they may be used as collateral and as guarantee reserves for banks.

Article 14: Anyone who counterfeits these bonds or damages credit shall be punished by the judicial authorities in accordance with the law.

Article 15: These regulations shall come into effect on the date of promulgation. (July 24)

Southern Route Bandit Suppression Army

Three Routes Launch General Offensive Against Jiangxi Bandits

The First Column Advances Towards Yudu

The Second Column Advances Towards Huichang

The Third Column Advances Towards Ruijin

A letter from Shantou on the 21st: The Southern Route Bandit Suppression Headquarters moved to Dayuling on the 15th, with Yu Hanmou concurrently serving as the headquarters director. The bandit suppression troops on each route also advanced on different routes from the 15th, with their destinations being Yudu, Huichang, and Ruijin. It is reported that Li Zhenqiu's division of Yu Hanmou's First Column has moved from Ganzhou to Shadi, Suichuan, and Wan'an. Peng Linsheng's two regiments of Wudao garrisoned Tangjiangwei to guard against Xingguo. Ye Zhao's division was dispatched to reinforce Xinfeng, and together with Wang Zanbin's troops stationed in Sannan, they formed a unified force, assisting Li Han's troops in Nanxiong as a reserve force. Huang Zhiwen's division of Li Yangjing's Second Column was stationed in Jize, Niudouguang, and Dazhe. Huang Yanzhen's division was stationed in Pingyuan and Meixian. Huang Renhuan's division was left in Yan to garrison the line from Yingyu Brigade to Wuping to Jionglong. Another brigade went out of Wuping and Yongpingzhai to raid Luotang and join forces with Huichang Yunmenling, with Huang Yanzhen as the central route, Huang Zhiwen as the right route, and Huang Renhuan as the left route, and is now advancing towards Anyuan and Xunwu. As for the Third Column, Qu Qingnian's troops attacked Changting head-on from Longyan Baisha, guarding the area between Liancheng Luokou and Beiwei. Liu Heding's troops moved out of Taining, northern Fujian, to attack the rear of Changting as the right route. Zhang Yan's troops moved out towards Qianjiazhai, Shanghang, to attack Changting as the left route. It is reported that the Communist bandit pseudo-commander Ye Jianying has moved the pseudo-teaching regiment to Huichang, preparing to fight against the Second Column. Yang Yuchun, the pseudo-Young Pioneer Division Commander, recently surrendered to Gui Zhenyuan Brigade of Liu Heding's troops in Taining. According to his confession, "The Red Bandits are now under pressure from all sides, and all their elite troops are concentrated on the Fujian-Jiangxi border, using the terrain and mountains for defense. In February of this year, the Red Army was reorganized in Lichuan, with three army corps under the First Front Army, four divisions per army corps, three regiments per division, and one special service company. Each regiment has three infantry companies, one machine gun company, three platoons per company, three squads per platoon, and ten to twelve soldiers per squad. Each army corps has an average of more than 12,000 soldiers. The 11th Army directly under the First Front Army is in Jinxi, the 12th Army is in Guangchang Nanfeng, the 19th Army is in Changting, the 23rd Army is near Qingliu Ninghua, the 22nd Army is following the First Front Army, the Independent 1st Division is in Xunwu, the Independent 3rd Division is in Qingliu Ninghua, the Independent 4th Division is on the border of Guangchang, the Independent 7th Division is between Changting and Liancheng, and the Independent 5th Division is in the mountains of Shanghang and Wuping, all of which are composed of makeshift Red Guards and have no combat capability. The Independent Divisions are in newly occupied areas and areas adjacent to the White areas, specializing in kidnapping and looting, and are responsible for guerrilla harassment work. All their members are local ruffians." The Southern Route Bandit Suppression Army is now advancing into southern Jiangxi, and the Air Force, led by Wu Jianwen, arrived in Meixian on the 12th. Another heavy team also arrived in Meixian. On the 14th, Deputy Team Leader Ao Lun flew directly from Guangzhou to Meixian and flew to the Fujian-Jiangxi border during the day to reconnoiter and assist the various armies in suppressing the bandits. Nanhui

Locusts Discovered in Various Townships of the First District

Recently, locusts have suddenly been discovered in the fields of Huangtan, Yihong, Zhu Nan, and other townships in the first district of this county. The township chiefs immediately reported this to the district office, which in turn reported it to the county government. County Magistrate Yuan believes that the work of controlling locusts brooks no delay, and he personally led the township chiefs of the district to various townships yesterday morning to supervise and encourage the farmers to do their best to capture the locusts, resulting in the capture of five large sacks of locusts. While capturing the locusts, he distributed simple methods for preventing and eliminating locusts along the way, advising farmers to unite and eliminate the locusts in a timely manner to prevent future troubles.

Old Man Rapes Six-Year-Old Girl

Gu, who lives in the Qimiao area of the Fifth District and is nearly fifty years old and makes a living as a bucket maker, took advantage of the absence of his neighbor Xia the night before and forcibly raped his six-year-old daughter. When Xia returned home, the daughter immediately cried and screamed in pain. Xia reported this to the Nicheng Public Security Substation, which dispatched police to arrest Gu. He also took his daughter to the Public First Hospital in the city overnight to request medical treatment. After examination by the doctor, the girl's private parts were found to be seriously injured. Yesterday, the substation presented Gu to the County Public Security Bureau for transfer to the county government for interrogation and prosecution. Suzhou

Sick Woman Suddenly Disappears in the Middle of the Night

Gao, the wife of Zhu Tianru, a rice shop clerk from Xiaomidu Bridge outside Panmen, is 33 years old. Recently, she fell ill and consulted Dr. Xu Bao'an. Dr. Xu, knowing that she was pregnant, was afraid that it would aggravate her condition, told her to rest quietly. However, at 11 p.m. on the 25th, Zhu Tianru woke up and found that his sick wife was suddenly missing from the bed and the front door was open. After searching in vain, the woman's body was suddenly found in the river at Xiaomidu Bridge at 9 a.m. on the 26th. It has now been reported to the court for an autopsy.

Wuxi

Verdict in the Embezzled Stolen Pig Case

On the night of April 12 this year, Yang Zuxun, the Fourth Jia Chief of the Teratou Town Security Guard in the Fifth District (Tianshang City), and others intercepted 36 stolen pigs worth on the side of the No. 3 Bridge on Xicheng Road and divided the proceeds. Later, Zhang Qisen, a trainer from the County Security Guard Council, went to the countryside to investigate. Yang immediately bribed Hu Bin, the Second Section Chief of the Public Security Bureau, to Zhang, which was discovered and they were all arrested and sent to the County Court. After the Procuratorate filed a public prosecution, Judge Guo Weiran repeatedly held court hearings and announced the conclusion of the debate. Yesterday was the date for the verdict in the case. At around 11 a.m., Judge Guo took the seat in the criminal court and signed an order to bring the detained Hu Bin, Zhang Qisen, and other five defendants to the court and sentenced Hu Bin to three years of imprisonment and a fine of 1,000 yuan, Yang Zuxun to two years of imprisonment and a fine of 1,200 yuan, Zhang Qisen to one year and sixteen months of imprisonment and a fine of 1,600 yuan, Ge Zhen to one year and eight months of imprisonment and a fine of 800 yuan, and Zhang Panquan to one year of imprisonment and a fine of 400 yuan. After the verdict, they were all ordered to be returned to detention. It is reported that Hu Bin and others will appeal.

The Dispute over Rice Industry Discounts Remains Unresolved

The County Chamber of Commerce of this county, in order to resolve the dispute over rice and bean discounts, specially invited 18 representatives of the eight rice industry sections, including Zhao Zixin, Li Zhongchen, and Tao Yinfu, to a meeting at the chamber yesterday to discuss a solution. Chairman Yang Xichun solicited the opinions of the representatives, and each representative spoke in succession based on their position and stated their reasons. As a result, the Chamber of Commerce proposed a compromise plan to overturn the 99 discount and the 984 discount and change it to a 987 discount. The opinions in the Sanliqiao section were somewhat accepting, while the attitude in the Beitang section was still extremely firm, with the aim of maintaining the original plan of 99 discount throughout. Finally, it was decided that the Chamber of Commerce would inform the Rice and Bean Industry Association to convene a general meeting of the industry immediately to properly plan a unified solution in order to avoid disputes and stabilize the business.

In order to reorganize the finances of the entire province, Shu Shifu, Director of the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance, specially rotated among the Commissioner's offices to convene finance meetings for the county magistrates. Changshu

Rice Stem Borers and Locusts Discovered in Shazhou

There has been no rain for a long time, and the drought is rampant. The farmland irrigation almost nowhere to draw water. The rice fields in Shazhou City in the Fourth District here, because the land is newly formed and naturally fertile, have abundant harvests. This year, due to the drought, rice stem borers and locusts have suddenly been discovered. It is observed that their momentum is spreading from Jiangbei. Zhu Qingnan, the district chief of the district, has reported this to the county government and has already issued a notice to all townships to take proper precautions and to do their best to eliminate the locusts in the affected townships.

Unidentified Male Corpse Discovered in Heyang

Yesterday (the 25th) afternoon, a male corpse was discovered in Shandong Tangwan, Heyang Township, Fifth District, wearing a blue and white short shirt and trousers. It appeared to have been drowned for a long time, so its face was blurred. It is said that this corpse was a fugitive in a major case, or a person who committed suicide out of fear of punishment. Xu, the district chief, has reported this to the county government, and it has been decided to send personnel to the countryside on the 26th for an autopsy.

Zhenjiang

Inferior Son's Robbery Implicates Elderly Mother

In Lane 11, Daogjia Lane, Chaosui Ditch, a local resident, Old Mrs. Gao, is over sixty years old and has no children. A nephew, Chen Zhaoyuan, lives with his wife in Old Mrs. Gao's house. Chen used to work as a tea server on the Yuantai tugboat of the Tiantai Company but is now unemployed. Next door to Old Mrs. Gao lives Old Mrs. Yuan, who is in her fifties and became a widow at a young age, relying on her own labor to make a living and raise her son, Jiaxiang. She recommended him to work in a lumber business in Bengbu, but he was later dismissed due to poor conduct and returned to town. It was reported that someone knocked on the Gao residence last night, claiming to deliver a telegram from Hankou. Chen Zhaoyuan's wife opened the door, and Yuan and two others immediately entered. They forced Chen Zhaoyuan's wife into a water tank, but Chen desperately pulled his wife out. They were frightened and dared not make a sound. Yuan then entered the room and searched around the windows, but found nothing. Yuan and the other two then snatched a gold necklace from Old Mrs. Gao's neck and fled with shouts. However, two robbers were captured by patrol officers at the southern entrance of Chaosui Ditch and were sent to the Fourth Branch of the Provincial Public Security Bureau. It was revealed that one was named Ji Chun and the other Yang Zhigao. It was said that one was a tea server at a bathhouse. The bureau prepared a document to send the two robbers to the General Bureau for legal action, and Old Mrs. Yuan was taken to the bureau and ordered to hand over her son. Yuan's residence was also sealed off.

Wheat Prices in Jiangbei Expected to Rise

This year, the second wheat crop in Jiangbei, Jiangsu Province, had a bumper harvest, but the market price was extremely low. Top-quality Yuhua wheat was only selling for four yuan per stone, the next best for three yuan and fifty cents, and the rest for three yuan. Therefore, farmers were invariably worried. The farmers' associations in various counties sent telegrams to the provincial government, requesting the lifting of restrictions on grain exports, so that the surplus wheat in Jiangbei could be transported to other places for sale to regulate the market. Since this month, many farmers in Jiangbei have been transporting accumulated wheat to Anhui Province and various places south of the Yangtze River in this province via the Huai and Yun waterways. At the same time, major flour companies in Wuhan, Shanghai, Tianjin, and other places are also actively purchasing Yuhua wheat, causing the price to rise from four yuan to seven yuan. The next best also rose to six yuan and twenty cents, and the rest rose from three yuan to five yuan and sixty cents. Farmers in rural areas, seeing the active grain market and high prices, are transporting their accumulated wheat to the market. In a few days, grain merchants from distant places will come to purchase wheat, and prices are expected to rise further. Farmers in Jiangbei may have a chance to catch their breath.

Yangzhou

Antiquities Discovered in Lianjie Island

Lianjie Island in the third district of the county belongs to the collapsed river area. The ancient tombs there are all being relocated. A bone collector named Zhou Huawen recently found two pairs of jade bracelets, thirteen ancient porcelain bowls of various sizes, and eight ancient copper coins in a pile of bones in an ancient pit in the area. It is said that the jade bracelets are Han jade, and the porcelain bowls are from the Longquan kiln. However, the ancient coins are too eroded to identify the dynasty.

The public Wu Zhuang school land, jointly owned by the education bureaus of six counties, Huai'an, Huaiyin, Lianshui, Siyang, Yancheng, and Funing, and the Huai'an Provincial Middle School, was originally donated by the late Huai'an gentry Ding Hengfu. Since Ma You'an, Li Youbin, Shao Zizhen, Liu Zhenqing, Xue Zhong'an, and others contracted the land rent, disputes have arisen over the accounts. This year, the contractor Ma You'an again violated the agreement and sold the stored rice in the granary without authorization. This was discovered by the other four shareholders, who also found items such as an axe used by Ma to damage the granary door. Dissatisfied, in addition to holding a shareholders' meeting to study the matter, they filed a lawsuit according to law yesterday, requesting the county to recover the losses.

Silk Reeling Worker Commits Suicide Out of Shame and Indignation

Shen A'nv, a silk reeling worker from Shaoxing at the Xianglun Silk Factory in Tanglou, Hangzhou, was falsely accused of stealing clothes by her colleague Zhou Shouzi and was stripped naked in public. The Public Security Bureau telegraphed the Hangzhou Court to send prosecutor Chen Huaming and clerk Feng Yongnian to the scene for an examination. It was confirmed that she had drowned herself. The factory has sent the perpetrator, Zhou Shouzi, to the authorities for legal action.

Local News

Regulations for the Provisional Land Value Tax in This City

The regulations have been approved and promulgated by the Executive Yuan

Since the Shanghai Municipal Government decided to levy land value tax, it immediately ordered the Land and Finance Bureaus to organize a preparatory committee for the land value tax to begin preparing all the procedures for collection. At the same time, it submitted the collection regulations and the organizational rules of the valuation committee to the Executive Yuan for approval. The Executive Yuan passed the regulations at its 107th meeting and sent them to the Legislative Yuan for review. The Legislative Yuan approved the regulations at its 25th meeting of the Third Session, deciding that they could be implemented provisionally before the promulgation of the Land Law Enforcement Law. However, because the regulations are temporary, they did not need to go through legislative procedures and were returned to the Executive Yuan by the Legislative Yuan, which then ordered the Shanghai Municipal Government to promulgate them. The Municipal Government received the order from the Executive Yuan yesterday, and in addition to notifying the Land and Finance Bureaus, it is also promulgating the regulations and rules as follows:

Provisional Land Value Tax Regulations for Shanghai Municipality

(Article 1) All land within the commercial areas of this city shall be subject to provisional land value tax in accordance with these regulations before the promulgation of the Land Law Enforcement Law. The boundaries of the commercial areas shall be separately delineated and announced. (Article 2) The following land shall be exempt from provisional land value tax: (1) Land owned by the city; (2) Land used for public welfare and charitable purposes without any income, which has been approved for tax exemption by the Municipal Government. (Article 3) The provisional land value tax shall be paid by the owner of the land as registered with the Land Bureau. If the land is held under a perpetual lease, the tax shall be paid by the holder of the perpetual lease. However, if the land is subject to a pledge, mortgage, or fixed-term lease, the pledger, mortgagee, or fixed-term lessee may be required to pay the tax on behalf of the owner when necessary. (Article 4) The provisional land value tax rate shall be six per thousand of the assessed land value per year. (Article 5) The provisional land value tax shall be collected in two installments each year. The first installment shall be collected from January 1st to the end of February, and the second installment shall be collected from July 1st to the end of August. The Finance Bureau shall be responsible for the collection. (Article 6) The Land Bureau shall first inspect the topography and current market price of the land, and shall also refer to the land value reported by the owners to divide the land into land value zones. These zones shall be submitted to the Provisional Land Value Tax Land Valuation Committee for review, and then jointly announced by the Finance and Land Bureaus. If the owners have any objections to the announced land value, they may state their reasons and apply to the Land Bureau within the prescribed time limit for submission to an arbitrator. The regulations for the aforementioned Valuation Committee shall be separately determined. (Article 7) The collection of the provisional land value tax shall not be suspended due to an application for arbitration of the land value, but the land value shall be determined in accordance with the decision of the land value arbitrator. (Article 8) If the provisional land value tax is not paid by the due date, it shall be deemed as tax arrears and may be subject to prosecution and collection. In addition, a surcharge of five percent per annum shall be added to the amount owed, starting from the day following the expiration of the collection period. If the arrears remain unpaid for three years, the collecting agency may submit a request to the Municipal Government for approval to auction the land and its fixtures to offset the tax arrears. The remaining funds shall be returned to the original tax defaulter. (Article 9) The original land tax and surcharges shall be abolished for land that has already been subject to the provisional land value tax. (Article 10) Land within the provisional land value tax area shall be subject to land value tax regardless of whether it has been surveyed. However, if the land has not been surveyed and the certificate has not been exchanged, the land tax shall be collected temporarily, and a provisional receipt shall be issued. After the survey and certificate exchange, the tax shall be supplemented. The owner may apply to the Land Bureau to verify the receipt and deduct the amount paid. (Article 11) When land subject to the provisional land value tax is sold, the transfer tax shall be levied at two percent of the current market price, but the land appreciation tax and inheritance tax to be levied in the future when handling land transfers shall be

Mr. Feng also has considerable sincerity

Judging from the latest situation, this matter will be transferred to the central government's highest authority for discussion and resolution, because both Feng Yuxiang and Fang Zhenwu are members of the current central committee.

Li Liejun's Talk

The rumors that Mr. Feng has turned communist are definitely untrue, and there are no slogans opposing the central government. As for the military and civilians, they get along very well. Mr. Li also said that, in short, the Chahar Bureau issue can be resolved satisfactorily after further negotiations by various leaders.
