Inspection of Ancient Artifacts from the Forbidden City

They were neither damp nor moldy

Inspection will continue today and tomorrow

Yesterday morning at 9:00 AM, members of the Provisional Supervisory Committee, together with staff from the Palace Museum, began the inspection. It was stipulated that the inspection time would be from 9:00 AM to 12:00 PM in the morning and from 1:30 PM to 4:00 PM in the afternoon. The Supervisory Committee originally planned to hold a meeting at 2:00 PM yesterday afternoon, but it was temporarily changed to 5:00 PM and held at the Albert Building. The details are recorded as follows:

Personnel Present

Yesterday morning, around 9:00 AM, the inspection began. The attendees included Supervisory Committee members Zhou Ren, Chen Rui, Huang Peng, Yu Tongkui (representing Zhou Huanxuan), and Ma Heng (Director of the Museum and ex officio member), among others. Some of the supervisory committee members in the North Sichuan Road storage had not arrived. Others included Zhuang Shangyan, Li Yihua, Huang Pengyou, Song Jilong, Tang Youen, Zhu Deming, Zhang Mingtao, Fang Xinghui, Zhang Deze, Na Zhiliang, Liang Tingwei, Wu Yuzhang, and other responsible inspection personnel. Many of them were staff members of the Palace Museum, because the supervisors only served as supervisors, while the work of checking, opening boxes, packing boxes, and sunning had to be carried out by the museum staff.

Inspection Results

Yesterday morning, box-opening inspections were carried out. The inspection personnel were divided into five groups, each with eleven people. In the afternoon, the inspection personnel were divided into six groups, each with twelve people. The procedures were meticulous, and the security was very strict. The results of the inspection showed that the ancient artifacts in the boxes were neither damp nor moldy. The monitors were greatly pleased. Afterwards, the staff carefully resealed everything as it was, and each supervisor was invited to sign on top to show solemnity.

Supervisory Committee Meeting

Yesterday afternoon around 5:00 PM, all the supervisors gathered at the Albert Building for a meeting. They all agreed to continue the inspection today and tomorrow. If all the circumstances were the same as yesterday, they decided not to continue the inspection. They also formally suggested at the meeting to expand the organization of the Provisional Supervisory Committee. In addition to the existing Executive Yuan, Military Affairs Commission, Academia Sinica, Municipal Council, Local Court, and Palace Museum, they plan to add the Municipal Party Department and other relevant institutions and legal entities for joint supervision to demonstrate fairness. Various Trade Associations

Requesting Special Amnesty for Liu Chongwu and Others

Hao Peng's Release Should Not Reverse Merits and Punishments

Please Follow the Precedent of the Zheng Jicheng Case to Encourage Patriots

The various trade associations of this city, in order to rescue the patriotic actions of Liu Chongwu and others, have jointly petitioned the Central Political Committee, the Executive Yuan, and the Judicial Yuan, requesting a special amnesty be granted according to the precedent of Zheng Jicheng of Shandong, so as to encourage the actions of patriots and deter the courage of petty criminals. The original petition is recorded below: A petition for a request. Since Japan has been poisoning Liaoning and Shenyang and further occupying the four northeastern provinces, people with blood and Qi are furious and think of refusing to use and sell their goods, in order to reduce its trade with China and express the accumulated resentment of the world, showing a lesson to

One in ten thousand. However, there are greedy villains everywhere. The enemy uses cheap dumping as bait, and treacherous merchants take advantage of breaking the covenant. The act of acting as an accomplice to a tiger should be punished in the same way as helping the enemy and betraying the country. However, due to the country's weakness, the resistance war is limited to military strength, and the punishment of traitors is limited by diplomacy. Therefore, patriots rise up and organize themselves, hoping to use drastic actions to deal with treacherous merchants. However, their original intention is only to warn and does not necessarily want to harm their lives. Therefore, the result of the outbreak of such incidents is not as serious as the announcement, which is enough to prove that in punishing traitors, they still have a loyal and compassionate heart. On November 28, 1932, Liu Chongwu, Pan Hongsheng, Zeng Songshou, and others were arrested by the public concession patrol for warning Deyuanchang Foreign Goods Store. The case was litigated in the First District Court of the Special Zone. After research, it was considered that the previous Maochangxin and other cases were related to the defendants, so the defendants were sentenced to twelve years of imprisonment for jointly plotting to murder. Tian Shuiyang, who participated in Deyuanchang, was considered to have helped plot murder and was sentenced to six years of imprisonment by the court. We believe that the case of Liu Chongwu and others is similar to the case of patriotic youth in Beiping City assassinating Zhang Jingyao this year. Both are for the purpose of punishing traitors. However, in terms of the degree of harm, one is a deliberate conspiracy, and the other is only a warning. There is a difference in weight. However, after the Zhang assassination case in Beiping City, the court did not prosecute the patriotic youth. It can be seen that in criminal prosecution, the prosecutor should take the interests of the country as a prerequisite and have the freedom to plant and choose. The case of Liu Chongwu is located in the public concession, and the prosecutor has the right to prosecute, and is organized by foreigners. Of course, it cannot take into account the national policy. Since the mistake has already been made in the first place, it can only be remedied by special amnesty afterwards. We have inquired that in the case of Zheng Jicheng in Shandong, although the defendant had righteous indignation, it was still a family feud. After the court sentenced him according to law, he was still granted a special amnesty by government order. In the case of Liu Chongwu and others, their actions resulted in killing and injury, and the motive was purely to eliminate traitors for the country. It was not a private resentment or family feud. In terms of their bright hearts, they are even above Zheng Jicheng. Briefly looking at the case, they should be pardoned. Otherwise, if Hao Peng's betrayal of the motherland, with the words of a Japanese, is both tied and released, the patriots who eliminate traitors for the country will be imprisoned because of adhering to official opinions. This makes those who surrender to the enemy rewarded, and those who are loyal to the country punished. If the punishment is reversed and the people's hearts are exhausted, how can the country stand on the earth? Therefore, without considering the boldness, we beg that your court approves and grants a special amnesty according to the example of Zheng Jicheng, so that righteous people can still strive, and petty criminals will know the fear, which is really convenient for the public. China Table Tennis Company

Also Warned to Relocate

Negotiations by the Confederation of Mechanical Industries Granted Postponement Yi Yuan Stops Production Labor-Capital Dispute Resolved

Other Factories All Improve Automatically

Since the nine rubber factories of Yi Yuan, Tian Xing, Da De, Hong Da, Zheng Da, Shanghai Industrial, Da Zhonghua, Yi Sheng First, and Yi Sheng Second, and the Meiya Silk Weaving Factory No. 9 were illegally interfered with by the British and French Boards of Works, warned to stop work and relocate, the cases are still pending. Now, the China Table Tennis Company has also been warned by the Public Concession Board of Works and given a deadline to relocate. Currently, except for Yi Yuan Factory, which has automatically relocated, Da Zhonghua, Yi Sheng First, and Yi Sheng Second have all improved one after another. The China Table Tennis Company, in addition to improving, has been granted a six-month postponement by the Board of Works after negotiations by the Confederation of Mechanical Industries. The details are recorded below:

Warning Measures

The China Table Tennis Company at No. 19, Lane 849, Youheng Road, Hongkou, recently received a warning from the Public Concession Board of Works and was notified of the following measures to be modified: (1) Move the boiler inwards; (2) Build walls on three sides to ensure safety, and open a door to the outside for ventilation; (3) Keep the emergency exit open; (4) Rewire the electric lights; (5) Do not build tents in the corridor; (6) Do not store goods near the factory. These six items must be implemented within three weeks; otherwise, it must be relocated immediately.

Postponement Granted

After receiving the warning, the China Table Tennis Company immediately reported to the Shanghai Federation of Machine-Made National Goods Factories, requesting a protest. The Federation, upon receiving the report, sent Secretary-General Cheng Shouzhong to negotiate with the Board of Works. He was received by Mr. Hunter, a Westerner from the Fire Department. After repeated negotiations, the Bureau finally agreed to a six-month postponement. The Confederation also supplemented the conditions of the Board of Works: (1) Install lead skin on the roof; (2) Prepare emergency sand to prevent accidents; (3) Broken celluloid and debris should be placed in iron buckets. The company is also planning to rebuild a new house and is actively submitting the house plans to the Board of Works for approval.

Automatic Improvement

After the Da Zhonghua Rubber Factory at No. 1102, Xujiahui Road, was ordered by the French Concession Board of Works to relocate the boiler, the Bureau agreed to a postponement after repeated negotiations by the factory with the French Board of Works. After the Yi Sheng First Factory at No. 83, Binlang Road, and the Yi Sheng Second Factory at No. 31, Binlang Road, were given nine relocation conditions by the Board of Works, the factories reported to the Rubber Industry Association and the Confederation of Mechanical Industries for negotiations. The factories gradually reformed the conditions proposed by the Bureau and reported them to the Board of Works for record. Therefore, no problems arose.

Yi Yuan Solved

After Yi Yuan Factory at No. 1002, North Chengdu Road, was forced to close down, all the workers were transferred by the Social Affairs Bureau to resolve the following measures: (1) Yi Yuan Rubber Factory is forced to relocate and is allowed to temporarily suspend work for three months from July 1; (2) During the suspension period, the capital will subsidize each person 3 yuan per month for food expenses, and pre-borrow 2 yuan per month. The pre-borrowed wages will be deducted by the capital from the wages after work resumes; (3) Food expenses and pre-borrowed wages for July and August will be paid once on August 3, and wages for September will be paid on September 3. After the labor and capital parties were satisfied, they signed and resolved the matter. Tian Xing at No. 108, Lane 58, Qiqihar Road, Da De at Nos. 18-30, Lane 1222, Kunming Road, Zheng Da at No. 884, Taopeng Road, and Shanghai Industrial at the corner of Youheng Road, East Fair Road have also automatically modified their facilities and have sent separate letters to the Board of Works for inspection.

Petition for Negotiation

In addition to reporting to the Ministry of Industry, the Shanghai Federation of Machine-Made National Goods Factories also petitioned the Ministry of Foreign Affairs yesterday to directly protest to the Board of Works. At the same time, it sent personnel to various domestic goods manufacturers to inspect and provide guidance on any improprieties to avoid the recurrence of similar incidents. The Rubber Industry Association also plans to petition the Municipal Government for negotiations.

Information on the Negotiation of the Tiānchú Airplane

The seller has agreed to ship the plane back.

Central News Agency reports: The all-metal fighter plane ordered by the Tiānchú Monosodium Glutamate Factory in this city from the Junkers factory in Germany was assembled at the Hóngqiáo Airport. During the initial test flight, the pilot was careless and damaged two wheels and the propeller during descent. Because the initial test flight resulted in damage to the plane, Tiānchú Factory believed the responsibility should fall on the seller. Therefore, they negotiated through two letters, requesting a new plane. Zen Shing & Co., the agent handling the plane, immediately telegraphed the German factory to report the incident. The German side replied by dispatching someone nearby to investigate the truth and determine responsibility, as the factory and the agent company are still in negotiation. However, according to inquiries with the person in charge of Tiānchú Factory, Zen Shing & Co. has already replied, not denying responsibility for the damage, but requesting that the damaged plane be shipped back before a new one is sent. Tiānchú Factory, however, fears that the German factory will take the damaged plane away, repair and repaint it, and then ship the same plane back. The damage to the parts would not be noticeable to non-experts, which could cause problems during future use. Therefore, the factory is still considering whether to accept the seller's request.

Petitioning the Bureau for Increased Compensation

Making a Ruckus in the General Affairs Department

Dispersed by Police Detectives

The families of the victims of the Tú Nán Wheel, a vessel of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company (Zhāo Shāng Jú), have already been compensated by the company with one year's salary. Those whose compensation is less than 500 yuan will have the difference made up by the Jūn ān Association. However, some of the families, at the request of the Preparatory Office of the Seamen's Union, are seeking compensation of 1,000 yuan per deceased seaman and recognition of their children's education expenses. They initially requested this from the bureau through the Victims' Relief Committee, but the bureau did not respond. As a result, yesterday morning, a large group of seamen's families went to the bureau to petition, and damaged property. The details are as follows:

Families Arrive at the Bureau to Petition

Yesterday at 10:45 AM, more than 30 family members of the victims of the Tú Nán Wheel, mostly women, some with children, hired three moving trucks and went to the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company to petition for increased compensation. They first went to the Business Department to negotiate. The bureau staff stated that the matter was being handled by the General Affairs Department and was not under the jurisdiction of the Business Department. The families then rushed to the second floor to the General Affairs Department, crying and making a commotion. Several men even forced their way into the General Affairs Department office. Since no one from the department was there to negotiate with the families, and no representatives came forward to present their case, they simply shouted and wailed, lying on the floor.

Damaging Public Property Inside the Bureau

Seeing that the bureau staff ignored them, several of the petitioners entered the office and threw all the items on the desks onto the ground. They also smashed a coffee table, broke two panes of the department's glass windows, and damaged lamps and other small items. The department staff immediately came out to stop them and advised them to leave the office and wait for the General Manager's decision.

Police Disperse the Crowd

During the crying, commotion, and destruction, the General Affairs Department reported to Liú Hóngshēng for instructions. General Manager Liú then ordered Shǐ Wéijùn and other officials of the bureau's General Services to negotiate with the families, asking them to elect representatives to present their case and not to cause trouble and damage property. The families stated that they were requesting an increase in compensation to 1,000 yuan per person. The bureau's police, fearing trouble, immediately reported to the Fourth Avenue Police Station. At around 11:00 AM, a large group of police arrived and dispersed the troublemaking men, women, and children from the bureau, taking those who had damaged property into custody. They were released by the police after 12:00 PM.

Seamen's Union Discusses

The bureau provides compensation of 500 yuan per deceased worker, as has been the practice in past incidents, and has not been stingy. Compared to other shipping companies, this is considered a preferential treatment. Now, the families are petitioning for increased compensation and also requesting education expenses, which is considered an excessive demand. The bureau officials could only offer reassurances and promised to reply after consulting with the Preparatory Office of the Seamen's Union. Yesterday, General Manager Liú dispatched personnel to the Preparatory Office of the Seamen's Union to discuss the matter. It is reported that the seamen's families also went to the Seamen's Union to request their assistance.

Abolish the Steamboat Comprador System

China Merchants Begins Pilot Implementation

Replacing Business Agents with Stewards on the Pǔ ān and Xīn Míng

Decides to Hire Foreign Instructors to Teach Specialized Subjects

In China, steamboats have traditionally entrusted the cargo handling and passenger service aspects to business agents (compradors), who are not managed by the shipowners. This abnormal system is unheard of in the global shipping industry. As a result, the authority of the crew and business affairs is separated. Furthermore, an excessive number of stewards and servants are hired, which hinders navigation and disturbs passengers. Therefore, the Ministry of Communications has ordered Shanghai-based national steamboats to abolish this comprador system. China Merchants has already taken the lead in implementing this, but due to the significant impact, it will start with a pilot program.

Ministry Orders Abolition of Compradors

The Ministry of Communications believes that in any country around the world, commercial ships, whether for cargo or passengers, are under the overall jurisdiction of the shipowner. The responsibility and duties are assigned to the chief and second mates. There are no separate compradors responsible for cargo handling and passenger tickets. Therefore, the authority on the ship can be unified, and the shipowner is fully responsible for the entire ship. Other crew members are responsible to the shipowner. Only in China, whether on ships in the Yangtze River or coastal waters, are compradors hired in addition to the crew. These compradors can freely collect security deposits or guarantees, and excessively hire stewards. Since these stewards receive no salary, they are forced to solicit tips and alcohol money from passengers. For example, stewards on Ningbo steamboats even hire assistants, who demand excessive fees, often leading to disputes. Often, the number of stewards on a ship exceeds the total number of crew members. Tracing the cause, it is all due to the comprador system. Therefore, reforming shipping affairs must start with abolishing this comprador system. The Ministry has ordered all Chinese-owned steamships in Shanghai to comply.

China Merchants Tries New System

China Merchants is now state-owned. Reforming shipping affairs is its leading role. After receiving the Ministry of Communications' instructions, General Manager Liú Hóngshēng immediately discussed with the heads of various departments the abolition of the system where compradors contract for business on the steamships. The company will take back the passenger ticketing business and handle it themselves. Zhào Yúntái, the head of the Shipping Department, had proposed this idea early on, but due to various obstacles, it could not be fully implemented immediately. After discussion, it was decided to use the company's top-tier coastal ships, Pǔ ān and Xīn Míng, as model ships for abolishing the comprador system and breaking the system of contracting for business. The company will re-establish the duties and responsibilities of the ship's internal operations and add a steward to each ship to be responsible for passenger affairs and the cleanliness and hygiene of the entire ship. Passenger tickets will be reported and accounted for accurately, and the authority will belong to the head office. On the ship, the steward will be under the jurisdiction of the captain.

Training New Talent

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company General Manager Liú Hóngshēng believes that abolishing compradors is imperative, but there is a lack of specialized talent to manage passenger services and maintain the cleanliness of the entire ship. Since the new system was implemented on the Pǔ ān and Xīn Míng ships, the results have been mediocre. Therefore, Mr. Liú proposed to the board of directors that training be given to service personnel and specialized Westerners be hired to teach trainees in the bureau, in order to prepare them for deployment on various ships to implement the new system. The proposal stated that in compliance with the Ministry's order to abolish compradors on various ships, the Pǔ ān and Xīn Míng ships were already being piloted. However, many of the company's river and sea ships still use the comprador system. The heads of each business are too focused on business matters and pay little attention to the various facilities and hygiene and cleanliness inside the ship, which leads to passenger dissatisfaction. The new river and sea ships that the company purchased with British Boxer Indemnity funds will arrive in Shanghai and begin service next spring. These new ships will, of course, follow the new system and not use business agents. However, China lacks specialized talent in shipping affairs and must train people in time to serve on the ships. The company should hire one or two specialized Westerners in shipping affairs to recruit trainees within the bureau, who will be taught the knowledge of ship management to replace the compradors. The board of directors has already approved General Manager Liú's proposal to hire specialized Westerners to train specialized talent in the bureau.

Panic Among Stewards

The Xīn Míng ship is a top-tier vessel on the North Sea route, and it has many stewards and servants. After the resignation of Business Manager Xie, the bureau took over the cargo handling and passenger ticketing services and stopped assigning business agents. Instead, a new system was being tested, and Mr. Chen was appointed as steward, reporting directly to the bureau. However, most of the ship's stewards have paid security deposits and were hired by the former business agent. They also do not receive wages and rely entirely on collecting tips from passengers for their livelihood. There are many of them. Now, it is heard that the bureau is changing the system and plans to change the stewards to a wage system, not collecting security deposits, limiting the number of stewards, and prohibiting them from soliciting tips from passengers. The stewards on the ship are panicking because they are worried about the reduction in the number of positions and the impact on their livelihood. Yesterday morning, they sent representatives to the bureau to inquire, but there has been no news.

Supervisory Committee Member

Gāo Yīhán Arrives in Bǎoshān to Inspect the Seawall

Gāo Yīhán, a supervisory committee member of the Supervisory Yuan, arrived in Bǎoshān yesterday afternoon to inspect the seawall. He was accompanied by Magistrate Jīn, Wǎn Zhīrèn, and local figures such as Táo Yúnshí. At around 4:00 PM, they returned to the city. Representatives from various agencies and local figures held a meeting at the Custody of Abandoned Properties to welcome him and presented him with a summary of their concerns. Wáng Zòuyún and Pān Mèngqiào, members of the seawall protection committee, and Liú Pǔzhēn, a member of the Party Committee, successively described the dangerous condition of the seawall. The autumn floods and high tides are imminent, and if substantial funds are not allocated for preventive measures, the consequences will be unimaginable. Once the seawall collapses, the disaster will be even worse than the floods in Hánkǒu and Gāoyóu in previous years. Supervisory Committee Member Gāo replied, explaining that the Central Government is paying close attention to the seawall and is working on securing funds as a fundamental solution. The immediate need is a temporary solution, and the provincial government has agreed to allocate more than 40,000 yuan first. Those present repeatedly asked Supervisory Committee Member Gāo to urge the provincial government to expedite the allocation. The meeting adjourned at nearly 6:00 PM. It is reported that he will also visit Sōngjiāng, Tàicāng, and other places to inspect the seawalls before returning to Nánjīng to report.

Sū's Troops Have Been Completely Repatriated

The 112 dependents of General Sū Bǐngwén, including men and women, were housed in two properties rented by the joint association of charitable organizations in this city at No. 3 and No. 25 Cǎishòu Lane, Jùlài Dá Road. After Sū arrived in Shanghai, the dependents were gradually sent to Běipíng and Hāěrbīn by ship and train. This repatriation has now been completed. The remaining dependents of Wáng Délín, apart from the 16 people sent away a few days ago, include more than 120 men and women living at No. 8 Hénglè Lane, Pǔshí Road, French Concession, and No. 5, Workers' Housing, Dàxīng Fāng, as well as 35 dependents of Lǐ Dù living at No. 17 Cǎishòu Lane. Therefore, the charitable organizations will move all the dependents of Wáng and Lǐ to the Cǎishòu Lane properties on Jùlài Dá Road for temporary housing.

Jianghai Customs Notice

Import Tariff Rate for Embroidered Linen Fabric

The superintendent and tax commissioner of the Jianghai Customs issued a joint notice yesterday stating that, in compliance with government orders, plain woven pure linen fabric imported specifically for drawn thread embroidery and other similar handicraft applications, upon proper certification, will be subject to an ad valorem tariff of 7.5% under item 104 of the Revised Import Tariff Schedule of the 22nd year of the Republic, rather than an ad valorem tariff of 25% under item 105. Furthermore, importers must provide a bond to the Customs in the attached form each time they import the relevant fabric in order to be recognized as having provided sufficient proof that the fabric is specifically for embroidery applications. All merchants are hereby notified.

Ship Collision Handling Association

Announces Establishment at Meeting This Morning

Adopting Detailed Rules of Procedure, Attached to the Bureau of Navigation

The Bureau of Navigation, in compliance with the Ministry of Communications' order, has formed the Ship Collision Dispute Handling Committee. The regulations were promulgated by the Ministry earlier. In addition to Bureau Chief Zhū Yàotíng, Section Chief Yú Shífān, and Assessment Section Chief Zhāng Guìzūn, who are ex-officio members, the committee also includes Xú Zǔfān, president of the Wúsōng Merchant Marine School, Leidingden, the harbour master of the Jianghai Customs, He Huijia of the Pilots Association, and Chén Gànqīng of the Insurance Association. The total number of committee members is seven. However, the harbour master requested to resign from the committee, which has caused delays. Bureau Chief Zhū Yàotíng has decided to announce the establishment of the committee at 9:00 AM today at No. 6 Sichuan Road and hold the first committee meeting immediately to adopt detailed rules of procedure and discuss handling ship collision cases. The committee will begin operations immediately. The address is attached to the Bureau of Navigation.

Mayor Wú Did Not Discuss This with Chairman Jiang

Initiated by Wáng Xiǎolài and Others

National Products Production and Sales Joint Corporation

A New Front Line for Saving the Nation through Production

Since the September 18th Incident (9/18) National Crisis, the people of China, in their pain and indignation, have deeply understood that in this era of economic struggle, unless they strive for production and strengthen national power, it is impossible to talk about seeking survival and avenging humiliation. Therefore, promoting national products and building industries have become the common goals of patriotic people. This is why the Shanghai National Products Company and the China National Products Company were able to become bulwarks on Nanjing Road after the national crisis, protecting the economy from outflow. However, national products companies are only a type of organization to assist in the promotion of national products and are not sufficient to create an organization that allows the production and sales sides to have full mutual assistance and full cooperation. Thus, the ideal of organizing a joint national products production and sales organization has become a demand in the advocacy of saving the nation through production. The representatives of various provinces who went to the United States in May to participate in the Chicago World's Fair brought their products to Shanghai, and all kinds of products were very popular among both Chinese and foreign people in Shanghai. They felt that the failure of various products to circulate was due to the lack of a liaison organization. Therefore, the representatives of products from Jiāngxī, Húnán, Jiāngsū, Fújiàn and other provinces Zhou Guànhóng, Wáng Sōngyóu, Shào Déhuī, Liǔ Hòumín, Zhāng Wéndì, Wáng Shìjié, Dǒng Kūnfán, Wú Guǎngzhì, etc., before going abroad, requested Lín Kānghóu, chairman of the National General Chamber of Commerce, Wáng Xiǎolài, chairman of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, and industrialists Wū Zhìháo, bankers Wáng Bóyuán, etc., to initiate the organization of the China National Products Production and Sales Joint Corporation, wanting to use the union of national products production and sales cooperation as a guide, to create a new front line for saving the nation through production. Wáng Xiǎolài, Lín Kānghóu, Wū Zhìháo, Wáng Bóyuán, etc., all agreed with his proposal, so they set up a preparatory office in the Níngbō Industrial Bank Building, and publicly elected Wáng Xiǎolài as the chief director of the preparatory office, Lín Kānghóu and Wū Zhìháo as the deputy directors, Wáng Bóyuán, Lù Qíshēng, Rèn Jīngpín, Wáng Sōngyóu, Wáng Sōngpǔ, Wú Guǎngzhì, Liǔ Hòumín, Dǒng Kūnfán, as preparatory committee members, and Zhū Déchāo as the secretary-general, to jointly plan and carry out the work. Later, in order to strive for rapid progress in the handling of affairs, the preparatory committee meeting reorganized the secretariat, invited Lín Wànláng as the director of the secretariat, and Wáng Píngnán, Wáng Jiàn'é, Wú Guǎngzhì, Zhū Déchāo, Guō Yǒngxī, Rèn Jīngpín, as secretaries, to handle the preparatory work separately.

Enthusiastic Participation in the Initiative

Since the China National Products Production and Sales Joint Corporation began preparations, enthusiastic people from all walks of life have joined the organization after hearing the news. As of yesterday, in addition to Wáng Xiǎolài, Lín Kānghóu, Wū Zhìháo, and the representatives of various provinces who participated in the Chicago World's Fair, those who have signed up to participate in the initiative include Shǐ Liàngcái, Zhāng Gōngquán, Chén Guāngfǔ, Liú Hóngshēng, Sòng Zǐliáng, Xǔ Shìyīng, Zhuāng Sōngfǔ, Yú Qiàqīng, Jīn Tíngsūn, Xú Xīnlì, Yú Zuǒtíng, Wú Yùnzāi, Lǐ Míngyáng, Yè Fúxiāo, Wú Wèirú, Xú Yǒngzuò, Lù Bóhóng, Xú Màotáng, Guō Shùn, Jīn Hóuchéng, Féng Zhòngqīng, Xuē Dǔbì, Pān Gōngzhǎn, Zhāng Zhúpíng, Yán Fāng, Jiāng Yīpíng, Wáng Bīnyàn, Cài Wújì, Xǔ Tíngzuǒ, Hú Xīwéi, Lǐ Wànlǐ, Chǔ Huisēng, Wáng Bódù, Zhōu Bāngjùn, Chén Shéngwǔ, Yú Guózhēn, Xiàng Shéngwǔ, Zhèng Chéngqīng, Zhū Wénqǐ, Wū Zhìhé, Yè Róngjūn, Hóng Rén, Zhuō Yǔtíng, Wū Yúnchéng, Chén Yìzhōu, Wū Tǐngshēng, Jiāng Zhèngchán, Xú Chūnróng, Cáo Guóhuá, Lú Chéngzhāng, Wáng Zhòngyuán, Yè Dàoyuān, Lín Wànláng, Yáng Yǒngnián, Wáng Píngnán, Hú Shūrén, Rèn Jīngpín, Wáng Hónglái, Sūn Jílán, Hóng Jīngshān, Wáng Jiàn'é, Qín Shànbǎo, Wāng Bǎotáng, Chuán Fāngtíng, Zhū Déchāo, Lù Qíshēng, and dozens of others. It is expected that even more enthusiastic supporters of national products will participate when the founders' meeting is convened.

Banquet of the Bankers' Association

Wáng Xiǎolài, Lín Kānghóu, and Wū Zhìháo, the directors of the preparatory committee of the China National Products Production and Sales Joint Corporation, held a banquet yesterday at the Bankers' Association to report on the aims of the company's organization. Those who attended included Kǒng Yōngzhī and Sòng Hànzhāng, as well as dozens of others. During the banquet, Wáng Xiǎolài, Lín Kānghóu, Wū Zhìháo, Xuē Dǔbì, and Chǔ Huisēng expressed their views one after another. Finally, Rèn Jīngpín, on behalf of the secretariat, reported on the company's operating guidelines. Everyone enjoyed themselves until over 10 p.m. before dispersing.

Wáng Xiǎolài's Speech

In this period of severe national crisis,

Some people may dislike our call to promote national products as a way to save the nation through production as too slow. But it is better to act than to do nothing if we only blame the slowness and have no other quick way to save the nation to implement. And this kind of slow effort is the fundamental work of developing the economy and building strength. It can cultivate the source of donations for the righteous army resisting the enemy in the front, and it can be the strong backing for the government to prolong its resistance and construction. If all the people of the country can earnestly work to produce and save the country, then the day of revenge and washing away humiliation will not be far away. The purpose of our initiating the organization of the China National Products Production and Sales Joint Corporation is to combine the producers and sellers of national products into one, not only to make the local products and products of various provinces unhindered in circulation, but also to enable the local products and products of various provinces to increase production and improve and progress, and to stabilize the lives of people in various places. In the future, we will gradually proceed to make all provinces and regions have branch companies, and be able to help each other and seek to develop together, in order to achieve the goal of saving the country through production. Therefore, this kind of company is not purely profit-oriented, but wants to use the power of mutual assistance and cooperation to promote the idea of saving the country through industry and commerce. We hope that people from all walks of life will enthusiastically participate, and if not, please give us criticism from time to time so that we can follow it.

Lín Kānghóu's Speech

The motivation for us to initiate the organization of the China National Products Production and Sales Joint Corporation really began with the proposal of the representatives of various provinces who went to the United States to participate in the Chicago World's Fair. After the various products from various provinces participating in the Chicago World's Fair were shipped to Shanghai, they were very popular among both Chinese and foreign people in Shanghai. If this organization had existed before, then these products would have been sold in Shanghai long ago. Recently, I received a report from the representatives who went to the United States to participate in the Chicago World's Fair that the average number of visitors to the China Pavilion at the conference was more than 15,000 per day, and many people were happy to buy various specially made products, such as Jiangxi porcelain, Yixing pottery, Fujian lacquerware, and Hunan embroidery, and so on, have already telegraphed for more. It can be seen that it is also very possible to promote national products abroad. In the past, no one organized an agency to pay attention to international trade, which not only reduced many figures in our country's foreign trade statistics, but also made the people of the country lose many opportunities for production. There are also many patriots and enthusiastic overseas Chinese who want to purchase national products, but are suffering from not knowing what is national products and where national products can be obtained. All these are because there is no joint organization between producers and sellers, which drives the people of the country to buy foreign goods. This time, we have approved the motivation of the representatives of various provinces who participated in the Chicago World's Fair to initiate the organization of the China National Products Production and Sales Joint Corporation, so that the domestic and foreign countries can increase the benefits of national production and purchasing power, and not sit idly by and miss them.

Wu Zhihao's Speech

Ladies and gentlemen present today are all founders of this company, and also esteemed seniors who have always been enthusiastic in supporting industry. There are many ways to save the country. The most significant include food, national defense, economy, education, and water conservancy, but the most needed is still the economy. This is because all the above aspects require the support of economic power. Currently, the state of the nation faces external threats from powerful enemies and internal troubles such as rural bankruptcy, foreign goods invading the market, the decline of domestic products, and the entire financial system trending towards depletion. If we do not urgently seek relief, the people will be impoverished and the wealth exhausted, and how can we survive? Recently, patriotic individuals have been striving to manage the economy as a way to save the country, such as revitalizing rural areas, improving silk and tea, developing the fishing industry, and promoting domestic goods. From top to bottom, we are working together and actively proceeding. The significance of our company's preparation and organization is to contribute our meager efforts to serve the country. Gentlemen, with your well-thought-out plans, you will surely have excellent plans to offer at any time, and we will proceed in sequence. I would also like to contribute my humble opinion to all of you. Our country has vast lands and abundant resources, but due to inconvenient transportation, insufficient economy, and conservative commerce, the products of various provinces cannot circulate among each other, resulting in some goods being abandoned on the ground, and others being blocked and accumulated. At the same time, there is a lack of domestic industry to supply the needs of various regions, and supply and demand do not match, causing the import of foreign goods to gradually increase. Therefore, our company is connecting enthusiastic people from all walks of life, searching for specialized talents, and gathering economic strength to unite producers and consumers, so that the supply and demand of domestic products can be met. Our company will cooperate with economic talents and industries to implement the following tasks: (1) Assist provinces and regions in establishing domestic goods trading firms to cooperate with our company to circulate products from various regions; (2) Assist factories by providing economic and talent support, supplying raw materials on one hand and improving products on the other hand to reduce costs and improve product quality; (3) Pay attention to international trade, as we often hear of the patriotism of overseas Chinese, which is no less than that of people in the country. Because there is no domestic goods supply as much as possible, they have to purchase foreign goods. Therefore, our company will contact overseas Chinese to organize trading firms so that domestic goods can be sold abroad smoothly. Other aspects include uniting the financial community to set up domestic goods warehouses and domestic goods pledge financing businesses, contributing to the government to implement protective tariffs, and promoting transportation to facilitate transport, and requesting the government to provide protection for goods along the way. All of the above are the business of our company, and we will proceed in sequence after the company is established. However, this matter is of great importance, and it is necessary to gather enthusiastic people from home and abroad, and work together to achieve success. I also hope that all of you present today, as well as the founders who have not attended, will introduce more enthusiastic people to participate in the initiation to strengthen the foundation and facilitate progress.

Xue Dubi's Speech

Promoting domestic goods has been a loud cry for the past twenty years, but because of the lack of vigorous implementation, no results have been seen, resulting in the outflow of money, the influx of foreign goods, and the decline of domestic goods, creating a situation of economic hardship for the people. In fact, commercial competition is an invisible economic war between countries, which must be organized and connected to have a chance of winning. Otherwise, individual battles will inevitably result in being defeated one by one. The China National Products Production and Marketing Joint Company is a new organization and a new front for China to conduct commercial warfare with foreign countries, enabling both production and marketing parties to cooperate fully and jointly respond to the war. It is a major need in modern economic competition. The use of this organization will not only promote the smooth sale of domestic goods and have a good effect on resisting the invasion of foreign goods, but also enable the progress of domestic goods production and increase production to help unemployed farmers and workers stabilize their lives, so that the national strength can be stabilized and move towards enrichment, to meet the needs of the government's long-term resistance. Therefore, to save the country, to save the poor, and to seek revenge, we must all do our best to participate in this organization and complete this organization.

Chu Huiseng's Speech

Mr. Wang Xiaolai, Mr. Lin Kanghou, and Mr. Wu Zhihao have initiated the China National Products Production and Marketing Joint Company to seek mutual assistance and mutual benefits for both production and marketing parties. This is the most valuable work in the year of domestic goods. From the perspective of production, it is not enough to set up a factory to fulfill the promotion of domestic goods. It is only necessary to pay close attention to raw materials. For example, in the case of cigarettes, there are many domestic cigarette factories in China, but 70% to 80% of the raw materials are still foreign goods, and only 20% to 30% are domestic raw materials. If we can replace these 70% to 80% of the raw materials with domestic goods, we will surely be able to help the development of agriculture and increase the harvest of farmers. However, due to the lack of close contact between the factories, they have failed to make overall plans. For example, there are many domestic goods factories that are similar to foreign goods or Japanese goods. Because Japanese goods are depreciated and dumped, they are often affected. Because Japanese merchants have government and banking support, they have support for advancement and retreat. Chinese factories often feel a lack of this kind of support. We very much hope that the company will be established as soon as possible and be able to create this kind of support for domestic goods factories under the cooperation and control of production and marketing, so that domestic goods can compete with foreign goods.

The Ministry of Industry

Director of the Jiangsu-Zhejiang Fisheries Bureau Changed

Chen Zhongsheng resigned

Yuan Lianghua takes over

Takes office at the end of the month

According to the Central News Agency, Mr. Chen Zhongsheng, counselor of the Ministry of Industry, has been serving concurrently as the director of the Jiangsu-Zhejiang Regional Fisheries Administration of the Ministry of Industry since January of this year. More than half a year has passed in an instant. Director Chen also resigned from his concurrent post because of the difficulty in handling affairs. The Ministry of Industry has appointed Yuan Lianghua to succeed him. According to Director Chen's statement of resignation reasons and the recent situation of the bureau, excerpts are as follows:

Reasons for Resignation

Since its establishment, the Jiangsu-Zhejiang Regional Marine Fisheries Administration of the Ministry of Industry has been in existence for several years, with a wide range of jurisdiction and important business. Since the Minister Chen of the Ministry of Industry took office, he immediately thought of re-organizing the past achievements of the bureau, hoping to make everything perfect, so that the fisheries of our country can have significant progress in a considerable period of time. He once intended to serve concurrently as the director of the bureau, but then changed his mind to have me serve concurrently because of the complexity of the Ministry's affairs. I was instructed to do my best to reorganize. After arriving at the bureau, I was determined to reform, and abolished more than ten offices and branches that had been established before, and reorganized the fishing protection patrol ships. In addition, the important cases in the bureau were sorted out one by one, and the matters that should be handled were handled in sequence. Although I encountered obstacles from time to time, I still struggled tirelessly. This time, the dispute over the collection office of the Fisheries Improvement Association was ordered to be handled, and it was also resolved peacefully. A few days ago, I paid a special visit to the Minister to report everything, and because the reorganization of all matters has come to an end, and I have been running around for several months, my mind and body are exhausted, so I have repeatedly expressed my intention to resign. Minister Chen has been kind enough to take pity on my distress and approved my resignation. I have now ordered the officials in the bureau to rush to complete the work.

Successor Candidate

Discovered in Caojiadu

Acute Cholera Epidemic

The Health Bureau has sent personnel to investigate

Engaged in injection prevention work

In the area of Caojiadu in the western part of Shanghai, cholera has been discovered a few days ago, and a total of six or seven people have died as a result. The Municipal Health Bureau learned that this kind of cholera will have a great impact on the lives of citizens once it spreads, so it has specially ordered the department to send personnel to investigate. According to the investigation report from the Third Department, this kind of disease is not real cholera, but an acute cholera epidemic. The bureau is now engaged in injection work to strive for prevention. Extra attention is paid to road cleaning and cold drinks, and personnel are sent to guide them to pay attention to hygiene. As for injection of the vaccine, since the beginning, it has been counted to have more than 100,000 injections. According to Director Li Tingan of the bureau to the reporter of the Xin Sheng News Agency, when the health cause was first started, most citizens did not understand, and only 30% of those who understood. After the efforts of the municipal government and the bureau to promote publicity, most citizens now understand the importance of health and cleanliness. Therefore, the progress of the health cause in the city has been quite smooth. It is expected that this kind of cholera epidemic will not spread.

Escorted back to his hometown by the orderly

Because he received a letter from his old mother at home, urging him to send money, I asked for leave to take my wife south. The accompanying person was an orderly from Shandong. At that time, I took several boxes of luggage, including several sets of Western suits for all seasons, more than 200 silver dollars, and many other clothes. Because the orderly had been with me for two or three years and was very honest, I let him go boldly. I stayed in Nanjing for several days to visit old classmates who worked in Beijing and talk about the situation after our separation. After a few days, I returned to my hometown, but did not see my wife and the orderly. I asked my old mother, but she had not seen anyone either. I was anxious and returned to Beijing, and inquired everywhere, but there was no news for many days. I was ashamed to go home to see my mother, so I came to Shanghai alone to look for them. I have not found them for many days. I thought that my husband and wife were very affectionate, and my wife would never run away with the old orderly. I don't know if the soldier had evil intentions and forced her to another place, or if there was another accident. It is difficult to know. However, the marriage cost hundreds of silver dollars, and now clothes and ornaments worth more than 500 silver dollars have been taken away. I have lost both person and property, so I had the thought of ending my life, etc. After obtaining the confession, the district chief ordered him to prepare a document and send it to the Public Security Bureau for disposal.

Li Shoushan died of his injuries

A Very Bad Habit of Smoking Red Pills Non-Stop

Uncle and Nephew Fight Over Property in Lawsuit

Dispute Over Shared Landed Property

Cai Fulin, a comprador for the British American Tobacco Company, is very wealthy. He has been kidnapped twice and ransomed with huge sums of money. Recently, due to property disputes, he is involved in a lawsuit with his two uncles, Wen Kui and Wen Rong. Cai Fulin's grandfather, Cai Qiuquan, married Ms. Yu and Ms. Xie as his wives. Ms. Yu gave birth to two sons, Wen Hua and Wen Yuan. Ms. Xie also gave birth to two sons, Wen Kui and Wen Rong. Wen Hua and Wen Yuan both died early. Wen Hua left behind three sons, the eldest being Fulin, the second Meilin, and the youngest Yunlin. In November of the second year of the Xuantong reign of the Qing Dynasty, Qiuquan passed away. Wen Kui and Wen Rong were still young at that time, while Fulin had already grown up. Therefore, not only did Fulin take over the position in the British American Tobacco Company left by his father, but even the estate was managed by Fulin. In July of the fifth year of the Republic of China, Fulin suddenly ordered the Wen Kui brothers and their mother, Ms. Xie, to move from their residence in Yongqing Lane, Xin Zha Road, saying that it would be renovated. However, Wen Kui and others later found out that the property had been sold. At that time, they demanded a share of the property from Fulin based on Qiuquan's will, but after investigation, they learned that all the land had been sold off over the years. Then they began negotiations with him, and it was not until July 10th of the eighteenth year of the Republic of China that an agreement was reached. On January 5th of last year, Ms. Xie became seriously ill and feared the worst, so she told Wen Kui that the ancestral cemetery was jointly owned and ordered him to inquire about Fulin to know how much jointly owned property there was. Fulin initially did not disclose it, and it was not until Wen Kui and others entrusted lawyers to negotiate that they discovered that the jointly owned property had been divided by Fulin with his younger brother Yunlin and Meilin's son Zhenyang in March of the seventeenth year. They believed that this behavior was improper, so they hired lawyers Wu Kaisheng, Tu Kunfan, Ni Jiong, etc., to file a petition with the First Special District Local Court, requesting mediation, but it was unsuccessful. Then they filed a lawsuit against Cai Fulin and Cai Yunlin for division of property, stating the location, acreage, and value of the disputed property, requesting that it be divided equally into four shares, with the two plaintiffs receiving two shares, estimated to be worth about 100,000 yuan. Yesterday morning, Judge Luo Chongtai of the First Special Court opened a court to summon them. The defendant Cai Fulin did not appear, so he ordered his son to appear with the second defendant Cai Yunlin to be questioned. First, the two plaintiffs, Cai Wen Kui and Cai Wen Rong, stated the intent of the lawsuit, and stated that what was previously divided was another part of the estate, and that the jointly owned land was not divided. According to Cai Yunlin's statement, the so-called jointly owned land is the company land mentioned in my grandfather Qiuquan's will. According to the instructions in the will, this company land should be inherited by our three brothers. Judge Luo stated that the case was complicated and ordered the two parties to collect evidence and reschedule the hearing. Municipal Social Affairs Bureau.

Preparing to Open a Public Factory

Relief for Unemployed Workers in War Zone

Central News Agency reports: The Municipal Social Affairs Bureau recently plans to establish a public factory in the Gaojing District. The latest developments are recorded below:

Greatest Purpose

The launch of this matter was still before March or April. The greatest purpose of wanting to run this factory is to provide relief to unemployed workers in the war zone. Since the January 28th Incident, factories in Zhabei, Jiangwan and other districts have almost been destroyed by artillery fire. Taking the printing industry as an example, 60 to 70 factories have closed down, with over 4,000 unemployed workers, most of whom are workers from the Commercial Press and the printing department of Labor University. Therefore, it was initially planned to open a printing factory in the war zone to provide relief to over 4,000 unemployed printing workers, but it could not be realized due to funding issues.

Drafting Plans

Later, the Municipal Government issued charity horse racing prizes, and the remaining funds were originally intended for the reconstruction of the war zone. Therefore, Wu Ya, Director of the Social Affairs Bureau, requested the Mayor to allocate 30,000 yuan as funding for running the public factory. The Mayor instructed to first prepare a plan and submit it for approval before making a decision. Director Wu then appointed more than ten staff members from the bureau to form a design committee to carry out the design. The plan has now been drafted and submitted to the Municipal Government for approval.

Surveying Addresses

The address of the factory has been surveyed and determined to be in the Gaojing Temple Public Village. There are more than 130 houses, built with funds from the Shanghai Local Association. It was originally intended to be lent to disaster victims in the war zone, but it was not suitable for use, so no disaster victims lived there. Therefore, the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau sent personnel to the Local Association to negotiate a lease, and the Association agreed to lend it. Personnel have been sent to take over, but it was stated at the time that the factory must be opened within six months, otherwise the Local Association will take it back. Since the takeover, preparations have been actively underway to open it as soon as possible.

Emphasis on Manual Labor

In the future, the factory will focus on handicrafts and will not use large-scale machinery. The purpose of opening this factory is to provide relief to unemployed workers, and most of the unemployed workers in the war zone are craftsmen. If machines are used, they must undergo training, and the number of workers accommodated is not large, which does not conform to the original intention of providing relief to unemployed workers. However, if the economy becomes more affluent in the future, it should be expanded at any time.

Before July 31st

Bring Export Certificate and Public Measurement List

Cargo and Passengers Transferred to Ganzhou as Substitute

The ship was carrying a lot of cargo downstream, and the draught was very heavy. The hull was already stuck in the shallow beach sand, so the shipowner repeatedly reversed, but could not escape. The passengers on board were also transferred to other ships to come to Shanghai. After reducing the load, it will be towed again. Today, the ship's export run has been replaced by the Ganzhou steamer from Shanghai. Whether the hull has been damaged or not will have to wait until it is rescued back to Shanghai before inspection.

They live together in Tangjiawan, Zhaozhou Road, like a couple. Later, Feng lost his job, resulting in financial constraints, so quarrels often broke out outside the house. They announced their separation in the first month of the lunar year and separated. Feng Jianying did not know where to go. Yuqing had to temporarily live with a friend surnamed Li at No. 15 Fuxinli, East Zilaihuo Street. After several months, she could not forget Jianying, and living under someone else's roof was not a good plan. Therefore, the idea of suicide suddenly arose. She went out the night before and swallowed a weight of raw smoke, and immediately returned to the Li residence. After being discovered, she urgently hired a car to send her to Renji Hospital for treatment, and died at two thirty in the morning the next day.

Gaochang Temple Ship Breaking Factory

Worker Killed by Machine

Family Demands Compensation

The Hui Ji Ship Breaking Factory, No. 93 Jiushanzhili, Gaochang Temple, Nanshi, specializes in dismantling all kinds of old ships. The scale of business is large, and there are many workers. Tan Shenghe, a worker from Hefei, Anhui, 25 years old, was in the machine room of the factory. At about 4:00 a.m. yesterday morning, he was accidentally hit in the lower abdomen by the machine operator's hand while working. He fell to the ground in an instant, and blood flowed like a gush. After being discovered by colleagues, they quickly ordered the engine to be shut down and went forward to check. Tan Shenghe's injuries were very serious, and his abdomen had ruptured. He died soon after. The factory staff reported the situation to the Gaochang Temple Sub-Station of the 2nd District of the Municipal Public Security Bureau nearby, and notified Tan's family at No. 508 Qu Zhen Shen Road, Xieqiao. After District Chief Jin Tiande of the 2nd District received the news, in addition to sending a patrol officer to investigate the truth of the incident and reporting it to the General Bureau for record, he also ordered the local security to report to the local court. In the afternoon, the prosecutor was appointed to inspect the body on the scene with the coroner. At that time, the deceased's brother, Tan Shengyu, appeared in court, took the body for coffin burial, and requested the factory to issue compensation to comfort the soul.

Second Special District Prison

Staff and Officials Fight in the Office

Candidate Warden Reprimands Foreman Warden

Slate as a Murder Weapon, Two People Go to Court

When the upper and lower staff, guards, and guards of the Second Special District Prison in the French Concession were established on August 1st of the 20th year, the Ministry of Justice transferred them from prisons in various places for appointment. After the former Warden Xie Fuzi was arrested for the case, the vacant position was taken over by Sun Xiong, who was appointed by the Ministry. Since Sun took office only two weeks ago, he has replaced the old staff, guards, guards, etc., and appointed more than 30 private individuals. Gong Hanbin, the leader of the third shift, 26 years old, from Jingmen, Hubei, was transferred from the first prison in Hubei when the prison was established, and has been in office for nearly two years. At 11:00 a.m. on the 25th, he led 20 brothers on duty. At 3:00 p.m., Gong inspected the prisoner's rooms on the 3rd and 4th floors at 1:00 p.m. At that time, Wu Bingyan, the candidate warden of the prison (45 years old, from Huangpi, Hubei, brought by the new warden, and arrived on the 15th of this month), was also checking all the prisoners in the prison. After Gong finished checking the room, he checked the letters sent by the prisoners' families on a small table next to the sports field. At that time, there were more than 300 prisoners exercising in the field. When Gong was checking the letters, he took off the hat he was wearing on his head and put it on the table because it was hot, and unbuttoned his collar to wipe his sweat. Wu saw this and blamed Gong for not being polite in his duties and for violating the regulations. Gong replied that it was hot and sweaty, and it was not a violation of the regulations to take off his hat and unbutton his collar to wipe his sweat. Wu reprimanded Gong for not obeying the guidance, and went back to the office to report the situation to the warden, requesting that Gong be dismissed. At 4:30 p.m. after the shift, Gong went to the 2nd section office to see Wu, asking what regulations he had violated that led to his dismissal. Wu replied that you don't understand the rules. It is appropriate to dismiss you because you were not properly dressed in your duties. Gong listened to Wu's words and said that since you, the chief guard, took office, you have never worn official public uniforms or armed belts, but often wear Zhongshan suits. Is this a violation of the regulations? I will go with you to see the warden for evaluation. These few words further angered Wu. He took a slate on the writing table and hit Gong's head and forehead twice, causing him to be injured and bleed, and his head and face were covered in blood. The two twisted into a ball.

After being persuaded by the people next to him, Gong immediately reported to the head of the Central Police Station. The head ordered Gong to be sent to Guangci Hospital for examination and treatment. He also sent Detective Zheng Jikun to the prison, arrested Wu, hung the slate used for the attack, and brought it to the police station for custody. That night, the warden learned of the situation and immediately sent the guard of the smoking ban office to the police station to protect Wu and try to resolve the case. The head of the police station did not allow it. Yesterday afternoon, the police station escorted Wu to the 8th Criminal Court of the 2nd Special Court. Judge Zhang Chaozuo questioned him. First, Yao Zhaodi, a lawyer from the police station, stated the case and filed a lawsuit according to Article 293 of the Criminal Law. Then, the detective reported the situation of the arrest of the defendant and submitted the slate used for the attack. The plaintiff Gong Hanbin also stated the previous situation, and said that he was dismissed without any reason, and he should not scold me in front of the prisoners, which damaged my prestige. Since the new warden took office, he has appointed private individuals, his uncle Cui Guangdao, his nephew Huang Bogang, Huang Mingjun, etc., more than 30 people. If our old colleagues have a very minor fault, they will be dismissed. The defendant has been in office for a short time and has dismissed many people in Caohejing. All his old colleagues are recruited and employed. He flatters the warden and oppresses us, and is preparing to dismiss our old people so that he can use his private individuals. When Wu Bingyan was questioned, he confessed that I found that the plaintiff violated regulations in his duties and was not polite. He did not obey the guidance and retorted. Therefore, I reported to the warden to dismiss him. Later, he came and hit me in the face from behind without asking why. Then, he hit me on the head with a slate. I did not hit him. I have been in office for a short time and have no opinions with him. I am completely performing my duties. The officer listened to the confession and ordered the court clerk to ask the forensic doctor to examine the plaintiff's injuries. Because it was past office hours, the forensic doctor had left. The court announced that the questioning would be rescheduled to the morning of the 29th. The defendant was ordered to reside in his current residence, and the plaintiff was ordered to go to the forensic doctor's office for examination tomorrow (that is, today) morning. The bailiff was also sent to the prison to entrust the warden, and the court adjourned at 2:00 p.m. After the case occurred, all the guards were indignant, so they all went to court yesterday to listen and were willing to testify when necessary.

North Jiangxi Road

Robbery Case Scheduled for Sentencing

Shen Chongli, a Chinese detective of the Hongkou Police Station, and Yang Zhaoqing, a detective, arrested four bandits, Zhang Defu, Chen Jinshan, Hu Xuekuan, and Li Fuxing, at North Jiangxi Road on the evening of the 10th of this month, and confiscated a pistol with five bullets. They were escorted to the First Special District Local Court for interrogation and detention.

After investigation by the detectives handling the case, it was found that the defendants had colluded with accomplices, held weapons, and robbed the two households of Liu Fu, No. 311 Dalianwan Road, and Gao Zhou, No. 313 Meizhou Road, of silver ocean ornaments between January 20th and March 28th of this year. They shot and injured the Gao Zhou, who died on the spot, and attempted to rob Wang Hexiang's property at No. 716 Lan Road. The case is related to the joint robbery of Jiang Shuncheng, which has been determined in another case. Yesterday morning, the police station brought Jiang, who was in prison, together with the four Zhangs, to the Criminal Court 3 of the Special Court. Judge Wu Zehan questioned them. Zhang Tianyin, a lawyer from the police station, stated the previous situation, saying that the defendants Zhang Defu and Chen Jinshan admitted to robbing Gao Zhou's family property on Meizhou Road at the police station, and Xiang, who was at large, shot and killed her on the spot. Gao Lan-ying, Gao's daughter, witnessed Zhang Defu at the scene. The Liu family robbery case on Dalianwan Road was committed by Chen Jinshan et al. The attempted robbery of the He Xiang family on Lan Road was also committed by Zhang Defu together with Zhang Ahe and others. As soon as they entered the door, they were about to search for robbery, but the owner, Wang Shi, shouted loudly to catch the thief. The rogues were frightened and escaped. The two defendants Zhang Chen also admitted at the police station. Today, the plaintiffs have all arrived in court, so they presented their handcuffs for inspection. Pang Na, a Westerner from the police station's pistol room, also presented a report confirming that the pistol was indeed the murder weapon that killed Gao Zhou. After Judge Wu questioned the defendants for a long time, he appointed a pro bono lawyer to defend the defendants and ordered them to be sent back to prison for sentencing on a scheduled date.

L Municipal Public Security Bureau Investigation

Wang Shuchiao Suspected of Assassinating Song

Follow Central Government Orders to Investigate Thoroughly

Bureau's Investigation Will Be Completed Soon

The Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau recently applied to the Public Concession Police for assistance in arresting Wang Shuchiao and Lin Zeruan, who were suspected of plotting to assassinate Finance Minister Song, but the Municipal Council opposed the transfer. The First Special District Local Court changed its approach and ordered the Municipal Public Security Bureau to produce the suspects in both cases, but limited their return within three days so that the police could continue the investigation. Later, because the Public Security Bureau took it away, it took a considerable amount of time to investigate everything, so it was not returned as scheduled, which caused dissatisfaction with the Municipal Council. The Municipal Council made a statement to the court the day before yesterday, but the Municipal Public Security Bureau believed that the Municipal Council seemed to have a misunderstanding of the situation, so

The bureau chief sent lawyer Zhan Jifeng, the legal advisor, to the First Special Court yesterday morning to explain clearly, roughly saying that the Public Security Bureau originally applied for transfer in the case of Wang Shuchiao and others. Because the police station

In opposition, the presiding judge ruled that the Public Security Bureau should take it away for three days. The Public Security Bureau was willing to comply with this ruling, and the lawyer also made this clear that day. The director expressed his approval very much. Later, he received a telegram from the Municipal Government to the Central Government, stating that the case was serious and complex, and ordered a thorough investigation. The Bureau respected the Central Government's order and conducted a particularly strict investigation, which took time. Therefore, it was not returned within three days. This has been communicated to the court by the Bureau, stating the reasons and hoping for understanding. As for the case of Lin, the Public Security Bureau

The investigation is coming to a close and can be resolved in a few days. In short, this is an administrative matter between the government office and the court, so there is an obligation to cooperate and assist each other, and there is no need to use means.

Special Report

Municipal Facilities in This City After the War (Continued)

E. Reconstruction Work. (1) Restoring Police Authority in the War Zone. Since the January 28 Incident, police districts 4, 5, and 7 under the Municipal Police Bureau had all become war zones, and the police could not exercise their authority. All district chiefs and police officers were first concentrated in the southern city, weeding out the weak and retaining the strong, and temporarily organized into squads 7, 8, 9, 10, 11, and 12, and a special squad. After the end of the war and the takeover of the Zhabei and Wusong police districts, the squads were assigned to serve in their respective districts, and the police authority in districts 4, 5, and 7 was restored. (2) Planning to Restore the Police Training School. The school was disbanded during the war a year ago. The Municipal Police Bureau is currently planning to restore it. (3) Adding Three Police Shifts to the Sixth District and Establishing Three More Police Stations. Due to the thin police force in the Sixth District and its proximity to roads built beyond the boundaries, the existing police officers were insufficient for deployment. Now, three more police shifts have been added, totaling three police chiefs and thirty police officers, and three police stations have been added on Youli South Road, Yidingpan Road, and Zhongshan Road. (4) Constructing the Seventh District Station to Supervise the Zhanghuabang Police Station. The old site of the station was destroyed by artillery fire. Now, three bungalows are being built on the site for the station chief and police officers to use as offices and residences. (5) Constructing Police Station Buildings in the City Center. The police station in the city center was completed in May 1933. After the Municipal Government inspected and accepted it, the Police Bureau ordered the second station of the seventh district to move in and operate. (6) Adding One Police Shift to the Third Station of the Sixth District. (B) Post-War Relief Work. (1) Employing More Officers to Take Important Positions. After the restoration of police authority in districts 4, 5, and 7, with the end of the military situation and the need to rebuild everything, full arrangements were necessary to overcome the difficulties. In addition to the original officers and police, ten officers, thirteen translators, and thirteen inspectors were added. (2) Establishing a Machine Gun Squad. The Public Security Police Brigade only had five squads. Patrolling and guarding were often insufficient. A machine gun squad was established in April 1933. (3) Purchasing Broadswords and Distributing them to the Police Brigade for Training. (C) Firefighting Work. (1) Zhabei District. The district has four fire brigades, including the Zhabei Fire Brigade and the Zhabei 1134 Fire Brigade. During the war, two damaged pumps and five hose carts were damaged, and about 60-70% of other items such as hoses,

hats, uniforms, and equipment were lost. Moreover, the brigade buildings of the third and fourth sections were completely destroyed by artillery fire. After the takeover, 12,400 yuan was allocated

yuan as a temporary restoration fee. Now, it is gradually being restored. (2) Yinxiang District. The district has two fire brigades, one in the town and one at the Hujiamuqiao Fire Brigade. The brigade buildings were not affected during the war, but daily necessities were looted by rioters. After the takeover, 2,000 yuan was allocated as a restoration fee. Recently, all work has returned to normal. Recently, the Hongzhen Fire Brigade added a new-style "Ketterick" brand fire pump truck to strengthen the fire protection capabilities of the district. (3) Jiangwan District. The district has one fire brigade, the Jiangwan Fire Brigade. Although it was on the front line during the war, the brigade building was fortunately not affected, but furniture and water hoses, fire engines, etc.

have been scattered. Recently, work has returned to normal. (4) Wusong District. The district originally had four fire brigades: Wusong, Wusong East District, Wusong Ning Shang, and Wusong Liangxi. During the war, due to intense artillery fire, the Ning Shang and Liangxi brigade buildings were severely damaged. After the war, the responsible personnel were scattered and could not be restored. Subsequently, the Municipal Police Bureau sent personnel to actively gather the responsible personnel of each brigade to discuss restoration methods. It was finally decided to merge the brigades into two, named the Wusong First and Second Sections Fire Brigade, gathering old personnel to serve in the brigade, and 3,100 yuan was allocated to restore it. (5) Zhenru District. The district has one fire brigade, the Zhenru Fire Brigade, which did not suffer major losses because it was in the rear. (D) Household Registration Work. Since taking over the war zone, clearing up household registration has been extremely important. After the takeover, the Municipal Police Bureau immediately dispatched household registration officers and police from various districts in the southern city to the war zone to distribute survey forms from house to house, register household transfers, add door numbers, re-survey and map door numbers, and draft new guarantee agreements, etc.

F. Public Administrative Matters. When the Shanghai Incident occurred, the affiliated agencies established by the Public Utilities Bureau in the war zone

and the municipal facilities, as well as the privately-operated public utilities under its jurisdiction, suffered the disaster together, without exception. (A) Affiliated Agencies. (1) The North Shanghai Street Light Management Office. Office equipment was completely scattered, and street light materials were

partially lost. They were slightly supplemented. (2) The North Shanghai Advertising Management Office has been completely burned down. It is temporarily located in the North Shanghai Street Light Management Office as an office location. (3) The North Shanghai Vehicle Management Office. Office equipment and impounded vehicles that violated regulations have been completely scattered, and the houses have been slightly damaged. They should be rearranged and restored immediately. (4) The Zhabei Shipping Office. After repairs, it was moved in to work. (5) The Jiangwan and Wusong Street Light Management Offices. The houses were completely burned down. After the restoration of power supply in Wusong Town, houses were rented to restore the Wusong Street Light Management Office. Street lights in Jiangwan have not been fully restored and are temporarily managed by the North Shanghai Street Light Management Office. (6) The Wusong Vehicle Management Office and Shipping Office have rented houses on Waimalu and moved

in to work. (B) Municipal Facilities: Street lights, standard clocks, and public advertising areas (three items). (1) Street Lights. There were a total of 3,450 street lights in the war zone, almost all of which were damaged. Now, in addition to trying to restore them, many more are being added. The total number is now higher than before the war. (2) Electrical Standard Clocks. There was a master clock and five slave clocks in the war zone. Two slave clocks were destroyed during the war. They have now been repaired and are operating as usual. (3) Public Advertising Areas. There were a total of 1,558 meters, most of which were destroyed. After reconstruction, 957 meters remain. (C) Privately-Operated Public Utilities. The privately-operated public utilities in the war zone include the Zhabei Water and Electricity Company, the Baoming, Xianghua, and Zhenru Electric Companies, and the Hutai and Songyang Telephone Companies. Among them, the Xianghua and Zhenru Electric Companies were not greatly affected because they were in the rear of the military operations. After the war, they were slightly reorganized

and restored power supply. The rest suffered serious losses or even fell to the point of being unable to maintain themselves. Over the past year, with the supervision and assistance of the Public Utilities Bureau, they have gradually recovered. The general situation is as follows: (1) Zhabei Water and Electricity Company. On the water supply side, it was maintained with all its strength during the war without interruption. The several trunk lines that were destroyed were immediately repaired and replaced after the war. On the electricity side, the poles and lines in the bustling streets have been sorted out. Currently, only the desolate streets of Zhabei and the Baziqiao area of Jiangwan have not been electrified because the scars have not yet healed and there are few residents. Therefore, reorganization has not yet begun. (2) Wusong Baoming Electric Company. Located north of Yunzaobang Bridge, which was a vital military location, the houses and machinery were extremely damaged and difficult to restore. The entire business area and franchise rights were then transferred to the Zhabei Company. The Zhabei Company is starting to sort out the poles and lines in Wusong Town and restore the power supply. (3) Hutai Long-Distance Bus Company. In addition to the lost vehicles, they have been repaired and resumed operation. (4) Songyang Long-Distance Bus Company. Destroyed almost entirely. The Baoshan County Government revoked its operating rights, and the Hutai Company took over the route. (5) Huashang Public Bus Company. After repairs and supplementation, it has gradually recovered. (6) Songyang Telephone Company. Completely burned down and impossible to restore. The Zhabei branch of the Shanghai Telephone Bureau immediately repaired and replaced the Wusong telephone poles and lines, and telephone service has been restored. (To be continued)
