Municipal Zoo to Open Soon

Tourist tickets: six copper coins for general admission, one yuan for annual pass

The opening rules for the municipal zoo of the City Education Bureau of this city are announced as follows. Opening Rules: Article 1: Citizens visiting the park should abide by these rules. Article 2: The park is usually open from 8:00 AM to 12:00 PM and 2:00 PM to 6:00 PM daily, but may be extended or shortened according to the seasons. It will be closed on the day after public holidays. Article 3: Citizens visiting the park must have tickets. Tickets are divided into general and annual types, and the prices are as follows: (1) General ticket: six copper coins per ticket (half price for children below the standard height). (2) Annual ticket: one silver dollar per ticket. Article 4: Students of various schools visiting in groups should contact the park with a formal letter from the school and are exempt from purchasing tickets if they are led by a teacher. Article 5: Personnel specially designated by various groups and organizations to visit should contact the park with a letter from the respective group or organization, and those approved by the park are exempt from purchasing tickets. Article 6: Visitors should respect public morals and must not engage in the following: (1) Teasing or catching animals. (2) Climbing and breaking flowers, plants, and trees. (3) Moving or damaging public property. Those who harm animals, climb and break flowers and plants, resulting in death or injury, or damage public property making it unusable, will be required to pay compensation according to the price in addition to being given appropriate punishment depending on the severity of the circumstances. Article 7: If visitors

find anyone violating the previous article and report it to the park, those who are verified to be true will be given free tickets to show the intention of advocating the protection of public property. Article 8: If visitors disturb public order, arbitrarily make noise, run and jump, spit, urinate, or have improper words and actions and do not listen to advice, they may be ordered to leave the park. Article 9: People with unclean clothes, naked feet, and those suffering from mental illness or infectious diseases that hinder public health are not allowed to enter the park. Those who are found after entering the park may be ordered to leave the park. Article 10: Visitors may not bring livestock, vehicles, and other bulky objects. Article 11: If visitors have inquiries, they may request answers from the park staff. Article 12: If visitors have opinions, they may submit them in writing to the suggestion box for consideration. Article 13: These rules may be revised at any time if there are any omissions. Article 14: These rules will be implemented from the date of promulgation.

Citizens' Education Center to Charge Admission for Night Garden

Issuing One Type of Long-Term Pass

To Be Implemented from August 1st

Since the opening of the Jingyuan section of the Shanghai Municipal Citizens' Education Center in the evening on the 16th of this month, the total number of visitors has exceeded 6,000 per night, with pedestrians crowded on the sidewalks and mischievous children frequently violating the rules. It is difficult for the night staff of the center to control the entire garden, and they cannot attend to everything at once. This is a cause for concern. Therefore, the 12th meeting of the center's affairs committee decided to issue one type of long-term pass to limit attendance. The quota is 1,000 passes, and sales will be stopped when they are sold out. After the approval of the City Education Bureau, it will be implemented from August 1st. During the day, visits will still be free of charge without admission.

The Xiamen Basketball Team Beats and Abuses Referees in Shantou Games

丨Shantou Sports Association Asks the Association to Issue a Warning丨

Dr. Yan Fuqing Discusses the Baseball Field

The Story of the Hospital Donation

Formal Donation Procedures Completed in September

Funding for Hospital Construction is in Sight. The Shanghai baseball field property on Route Père Robert, owned by the American oil tycoon Rockefeller, covers an area of more than 130 mu and is of great value. Recently, in response to requests from the National Shanghai Medical College and the Red Cross Hospital of our country, he agreed to donate the land unconditionally for the construction of a large-scale hospital and medical school site. This proposal is gradually becoming concrete. A reporter from Shenshi News specifically visited Dr. Yan Fuqing, president of the Red Cross Hospital on Haig Road, who is in charge of this matter, to inquire about the progress. We now present a detailed account as follows.

Origin of Land Purchase in Shanghai

Rockefeller, the American oil tycoon, is a famous American billionaire with vast properties. Throughout his life, Rockefeller has been generous in his contributions to public welfare and charitable causes. Rockefeller established a charitable fund management committee in New York, hiring prominent figures to form a board of directors responsible for managing all charitable matters funded by Rockefeller. These are divided into various committees such as medical and educational, which carry out their work separately. Various parts of the world have benefited from his substantial charitable contributions. Many educational and medical institutions in our country have also received assistance from him. In the medical field, institutions like the Xiehe Hospital, Yenching University, and Soochow University receive substantial annual cash subsidies. Ten years ago, he planned to establish a large-scale hospital and medical school in Shanghai and Beijing. Therefore, he specifically purchased more than 130 mu of land located between Route Père Robert and the Observatory Road in Shanghai, paying more than 700 yuan per mu, to begin constructing the hospital site. However, due to political and other changes, the project came to an indefinite halt, and the purchased land was temporarily lent to the Sports Advancement Association for use as a baseball field and other sports venues at their request.

Telephoning Rockefeller for Donation

The Wusong National Shanghai Medical College was seeking a new site because its buildings were destroyed by artillery fire during the January 28th Incident last year. Later, the college president, Yan Fuqing, managed to temporarily construct two Western-style buildings on the vacant land of the Red Cross Hospital on Haig Road to continue classes. However, the premises were small and insufficient. Moreover, the Red Cross Hospital was also expanding its services, and its wards, beds, and other acute medical equipment urgently needed to be expanded. Therefore, President Yan considered the vacant land in Shanghai owned by Rockefeller, which was originally intended for the construction of a hospital and school. He specifically requested that it be donated unconditionally to build another acute care hospital.

At the same time, the National Shanghai Hospital could also establish a more complete campus there. They jointly decided to prepare a detailed plan and telegraphed Rockefeller before the new year, asking him to generously provide assistance. After receiving the telegram, Rockefeller forwarded it to the Charity Fund Management Committee for review. After review by the board of directors, they agreed to the request because the land would be used for charitable and educational purposes.

Replying with Approval

At the end of last year, Mr. A. Gregg, Director of the Educational and Medical Group of the Committee, came to China to investigate everything. Upon returning to the United States, he reported his findings to the board of directors, who were satisfied with the results. In May of this year, they telegraphed back, expressing full agreement in principle and plan, with two conditions: (1) There must be definite funding for construction. (2) There must be defined operating expenses. If the above two items could be determined, the land would be allocated. After receiving the telegram, we began to raise one million yuan to carry out the construction and recently telegraphed Rockefeller, stating that there are already considerable means to address the two items raised. It is reported that after further discussion and resolution by the board of directors in August or September, the donation procedures will be officially completed.

Fundraising Situation

According to Dr. Yan's words to the Shenshi News reporter, it is almost certain that Rockefeller will fully agree to the donation of the land, which totals more than 130 mu. According to estimates by the Public Works Department, each mu is worth about 18,000 taels, for a total value of about 4 to 5 million yuan. It is planned to build an acute care hospital and a National Medical College site on the land. The construction cost is set at one million yuan, of which 800,000 yuan has been raised, and 400,000 yuan has already been received. The remaining amount should be raised in the near future. It has been decided that the hospital will focus on the treatment of acute illnesses, with the number of beds expanded to 500. The facilities will be as comprehensive as possible. The name of the hospital has been tentatively decided as Zhongshan Hospital. When building the new site of the medical college, the number of students and departments will also need to be greatly expanded. It is estimated that the college will need 500,000 yuan in annual operating expenses. In addition to the existing 200,000 yuan and continuing to request an annual subsidy of 50,000 yuan from Rockefeller, a subsidy will be requested from the China Cultural Foundation. In addition, a portion of the surplus land on the baseball field will be set aside to build civilian housing. The income from the real estate there will also help with operating expenses. However, the section on setting aside land to build civilian housing has not yet been approved by Rockefeller, but after our explanation by telegram, it should not be a problem. Therefore, the progress of the above plan is quite smooth. As for the start date of construction, it will be around August or September of this year, after it is formally approved by the Rockefeller Foundation.

A New Era in the Shanghai Lawn Tennis League

The China Tennis Club Wins the First Championship

Winning the 1933 Championship with 88 Points

Yesterday's Final Match: China Lost to the French Businessmen's Team 7 to 8

This Year's Lawn Tennis League Concludes

The Shanghai Lawn Tennis League Championship, which the China Tennis Club has never won before, has officially been won by the China Tennis Club for the first time. In yesterday's final match between the China Club and the French Businessmen's Club, the outcome no longer mattered, and new players were sent to represent the teams. The result was a one-point loss. This year's Lawn Tennis League has been declared over. The China Club had the opportunity to win the League Championship last year, but lost by two points to the Japanese Club. This year, their wish has come true, creating a glorious page in the history of Shanghai Lawn Tennis for the China Club.

Scores of China and French Businessmen's Team

(1) Zheng Zhaojia, Yu Tianguang (China) 6-1, 8-6, 1-2 defeated Meihan Sibailunzi (France) 2-1 (2) Tu Kaiyuan, Sun Linfang (China) 6-3, 4-6, 2-6 defeated Kelunnuofu, Gao'erman (France) 1-2 (3) Guo Yujie, Ma Anquan (China) 12-10, 6-2, 7-5 defeated Hui Aideluorenna (France) 3-0 (4) Li Nan, Qian Mingshu (China) 3-6, 2-6, 2-6 defeated Laopingsheng, Meilie (France) 0-3 (5) Chen Chuanzhang, Xu Demin (China) 7-5, 3-6, 2-6 defeated Futan Sishandousi (France) 1-2

Yesterday's Battle

Of yesterday's five matches, the first group performed the best. Zheng and Yu, two young men, cooperated wonderfully in many places. Zheng Zhaojia made many good shots in the first set. The failure of the second group was the most regrettable. The opponents, Kelunnuofu and Gao'erman, had mediocre skills, but they lost two sets to them. The third group, Guo and Ma, fought hard and won three consecutive sets, making them one of the best groups yesterday. The fourth and fifth groups lost because they were new players.

The Popularity of Four New Tennis Books

(1) Tennis Training Method (2) Tennis Tips (3) Winning Secrets of World Tennis Masters (4) Tilden's Tennis Technique

Qinfen Bookstore, 554 Fourth Avenue, British Concession, Shanghai, has published four new tennis books, which have become popular throughout the country. They are briefly described below: (1) Tennis Training Method, written by Ma Detai, tennis instructor for the 7th, 8th, and 9th Far Eastern Games. In addition to describing basic tennis training methods, the book selectively explains strategies for matches and winning tips. The author's experience is extensive, and his views are unique. It is a guide for learning. The book also includes more than 30 illustrations of posture demonstrations by tennis master Yu Tianguang, which are correct and beautiful, and extremely valuable. The price is 5 jiao, and the registered postage is 1 jiao 1 fen. (2) Tennis Tips is written by Bai Lang and translated by Wu Bangwei. The author, Ms. Bai Lang, has repeatedly won the American women's tennis singles and doubles championships and has a deep observation and research of the advantages of world-renowned tennis players. Therefore, the content of this book is a collection of the best of all schools. The discussion of tennis tactics is based on experience and the ultimate truth, expressed with more than 50 posture photos. The book ends with a description of the training process and strategies of a successful tennis player, which can serve as a model for those who study advanced tennis art. The translation of this book is smooth and clear, making it easy for readers. The price per copy is 7 jiao, and the registered postage is 1 jiao 1 fen. (3) Winning Secrets of World Tennis Masters, this book is co-authored by world tennis masters Mrs. Maddy, Jie Gubo, and Tilden. Each person explains their methods and secrets based on their own successful experiences, including what is necessary for tennis, how to practice, how to compete, how to improve skills, how to defeat enemies, and how to reach the world arena. Tennis lovers who read this book will surely improve their skills rapidly. The price per copy is 4 jiao 5 fen, and the registered postage is 1 jiao 1 fen. (4) Tilden's Tennis Technique, Tilden is recognized as the world's number one tennis master, with profound skills. The author of this book, Bo Sishi, is a famous American tennis coach who has a deep observation of Tilden's tennis technique. This book makes a general review of Tilden's tennis technique, so it is a compilation of the essence of studying Tilden's tennis technique. The book has a total of ten chapters and is accompanied by dozens of posture photos taken by Tilden himself, which are extremely valuable. The price is 5 jiao, and the registered postage is 1 jiao 1 fen. Tennis rules are 1 jiao per copy.

Special Article

Recent Living Problems of Japanese Primary School Teachers (2) Yuan () Ying

For further clarification, the number of teachers in each salary bracket is shown below:

Salary Bracket Male Teachers Female Teachers Number

Below 30 yuan 38 44 30 - 35 yuan 1781 3733 35 - 40 yuan 1469 3571 40 - 45 yuan 3982 12753 45 - 50 yuan 8956 11483 50 - 55 yuan 13466 7424 55 - 60 yuan 10838 4688 60 - 65 yuan 9799 2694 65 - 70 yuan 8408 1648 70 - 75 yuan 6845 1040 75 - 80 yuan 5654 72 80 - 85 yuan 5029 458 85 - 90 yuan 4424 220 90 - 100 yuan 5106 161 100 - 110 yuan 3611 69 110 - 120 yuan 2529 11 120 - 130 yuan 1756 4 130 - 145 yuan 1253 None 145 - 160 yuan 560 None 160 - 180 yuan 344 None 180 or above 334 None Based on the "56th Annual Report of the Ministry of Education of the Japanese Empire," published in January 1933.

The above statistics refer to primary school full-time teachers, and do not include substitute teachers, assistant teachers, and specialist teachers who earn even less than full-time teachers. The above are official statistics from a 1928 survey, so the initial salary for normal school graduates was 45 yuan for men in urban areas (or 40 yuan for those earning less), 40 yuan for men in rural areas, and 35 yuan for women. However, since last year, it has been reduced by 5% to 10%. The current initial salary is between 35 yuan and 45 yuan, so it should be even less than the statistics above.

As the statistics show, we can clearly see that most teachers, both male and female, earn between 40 yuan and 65 yuan. Teachers who maintain their lives on this salary account for 67% of the total, and those with incomes below 100 yuan account for 92%. Even those who earn more than 100 yuan do not exceed 145 yuan.

In addition to this salary, there are also additional allowances, housing allowances, and bonuses. Additional allowances generally require more than five years of continuous service and recommendation from the principal and school officials. They add 24 yuan to 48 yuan per year, 48 yuan to 72 yuan for more than ten years, and 72 yuan to 95 yuan for more than fifteen years (above is for full-time teachers in the core curriculum), as well as special allowances for those in remote areas (less than 36 yuan per year) or single-grade schools (less than 60 yuan per year). But this

type of allowance is not monthly salary, so assuming the highest seniority allowance of 95 yuan is obtained, the monthly average is only 7 yuan and 9 jiao.

The so-called bonus is 20% of the monthly salary every six months in Tokyo, which is 1.4 months per year. Rural bonuses are given once a year, usually 10% to 20% of the salary, but some bonuses are only 5 jiao. Many rural areas have recently been forced to abolish this type of bonus. Housing allowances are 7 yuan per month for principals (in the old city of Tokyo; currently, Tokyo has greatly expanded), 4 yuan for ordinary teachers, and 2 yuan for non-homeowners. In rural areas, it is generally 2 yuan.

In addition to heavy daily workloads, Japanese primary school teachers must also participate in extracurricular labor for social education, such as youth associations and maiden societies (mostly fascist organizations). The same extracurricular labor pays 20 yuan per month for two days a week at youth training centers, while tutoring night schools

also pay 17 yuan for two days a week for core teachers and only 8 yuan for specialist teachers.

Furthermore, a middle-aged teacher in a single-grade school in the mountainous area of Iwate Prefecture once expressed the following sentiments:

"Children and their parents also bring vegetables to the teachers' residence, so we often look forward to them. What a humble mentality this is, but there are so many children, and life is really too difficult. Recently, there have often been undernourished children in this school. Women give them something to eat at lunchtime, and they are very happy. The misery of rural life

has reached such a point!"

(3) Origin of Funding

Originally, the salaries of Japanese primary school teachers were borne by the national or local governments. When the local government bears the entire cost, the teachers are directly governed by the local autonomous bodies as civil servants. When the national government bears the cost, the teachers are directly governed by national agencies (government, local government officials). The affiliation of primary school teachers was not much of a problem originally, but what they longed for was to be able to guarantee their salaries.

Looking at the rural expenditures (45.7% of the 1931 rural expenditures in the 1933 edition of the Agricultural Yearbook),

6% is used for school expenses, of which teachers' salaries account for 28.89% (133 million yuan). However, since agriculture, the source of rural finances, has suffered from panic, the above expenditures have also become a problem. Akita Prefecture plans to manage school afforestation to seek a source of educational funding, but without using the funds for purchasing seedlings, the current salary arrears problem cannot be solved. So, it is also a case of distant water not quenching immediate thirst. Since the countryside is so poor, the only solution is to find a way for the national government to bear the cost.

Regarding the national treasury's burden of teachers' salaries, the "Compulsory Education Expense National Treasury Burden Law" was enacted in 1918, with the national treasury spending 10 million yuan annually. From 1923, it was 40 million yuan, 70 million yuan from 1926, 75 million yuan from 1927, and 85 million yuan from 1930. Last year, another temporary expenditure of 12 million yuan was allocated to poor rural areas. However, the current state finances of Japan are not based on income and expenditure, but on expenditure and public debt as income, with the "gold" finance transforming into "paper" finance. Therefore, the current source of funds is also in a state of flux, where it exists if you say it does and doesn't if you say it doesn't.

The so-called Northeast Incident cost 72 million yuan in 1931, 252 million yuan in 1932, and the budget for this year is 161 million yuan, totaling 486 million yuan, a huge sum. Furthermore, the so-called confidential expenses are not included. It is unknown when this situation will end, and Minister of War Araki has proposed a three-year plan to expand the army's equipment at 102 million yuan per year. The Japanese militarists disregard people's livelihood and only seek to realize their militaristic ideology. However, Minister of Education Hatoyama is also striving for educational funds, or is cleaning up the army to greatly reduce military expenditures, or is Qing Takahashi, Minister of Finance, issuing more public bonds, and does not oppose the national treasury seeking a guarantee of primary school teachers' lives. However, given the current state of Japanese national finances, even if the national government bears the salaries of primary school teachers, the problem of salary arrears cannot be completely resolved.

(4) Two New Trends

Under these circumstances, Japanese primary school teachers are reflecting two noteworthy trends: one is leaning to the left, and the other is a fascist tendency represented by Ibaraki Prefecture.

The Akita Prefecture Academic Affairs Department has also established a policy to crack down on the ideology of teachers and students, and the rules are recorded below:

(1) Investigate the ideological system of teachers and students, create forms, and store them in the county. (1) Set up inspectors to investigate the ideological situation of teachers and students in the county.

(1) The performance of fairy tales and other scripts centered on teachers and students in the school, as well as the editing of alumni magazines, must be approved by the school authorities.

(1) The principal must regularly report the ideological trends of teachers and students to the county government in secret. Those who delay or conceal reports will be punished.

(1) Regularly hold lectures on ideology and conduct individual guidance to people of note.

Another trend represented by Ibaraki is the fascistization of native localism, represented by the Feixiang Association movement of Feixiang, Zhejiang teachers. Although this trend is still in its infancy, the fact that elementary school teachers are at the center of loving their hometown and that elementary school teachers participated in the Blood Pledge Corps incident proves that it has already manifested considerably. (The End)

National Goods Forum

Promoting Domestic Products Through Government-Citizen Cooperation

— Yang Cang

Recently, the Shandong Provincial Government, local agencies, and people's organizations have established the Shandong Provincial Domestic Goods Promotion Committee, advocating for mandatory promotion of domestic products. All goods used by party, government, and military agencies and their staff throughout the province are limited to domestic goods. It is intended to set an example and foster good habits. This kind of government-citizen cooperation in the mandatory promotion of domestic goods is far more effective than simply relying on empty slogans and posters to promote domestic goods. It is worth remembering that since the establishment of the National Government, there have been meetings, official documents, and methods for promoting domestic goods, which can be said to have emphasized promotion to the utmost. However, there has been little effect in recent years. Government personnel have higher incomes and higher living standards, and all they seek is comfort and enjoyment. What time do they have to ask whether the items they use are domestic? It is said that "the higher the position of government personnel, the more they promote foreign goods." What a heartbreaking thing this is. They even abandon excellent local products and prefer foreign goods, thinking that it is advantageous. Recently, Mrs. Yu Yingjie talked about how there are many domestic products in China that cost less than half the price of foreign goods, the only difference being the packaging and style. If they were properly guided and improved, why would their sales be entirely taken over by foreign goods? Her words are even more insightful. The recent Shandong Domestic Goods Exhibition promotes domestic goods, starting with local products in the province, such as the colored glaze from Boshan and the crepe satin from Yantai. We should first promote them and distribute them to various places to expand the market for promotion. This spirit of government-citizen cooperation is highly commendable. We hope that other provinces will follow suit and that provincial governments will order county governments to do the same. If we can implement it sincerely and cooperate thoroughly, then the development of domestic goods is very promising.

National Products Introduction

The National Product Handkerchief Factory that Dominates Southern China

— Zhou Ling

Since China opened its doors and traded with foreign countries, all overseas goods have been concentrated in our country's markets, so the commercial war has become even more fierce. Good things will definitely win, and bad things will definitely fail. This is a definite principle. It is a pity that our country's industry has not made long-term progress. The goods that are imported increase year by year. Everyone likes to buy them, and the people's lives are becoming increasingly difficult. In recent years, educated people in our country have used the principles of machine industry to set up factories to manufacture goods in order to remedy the situation. For example, handkerchiefs, although very small, are widely sold. Men and women in society must have one, so handkerchiefs have become necessities. Unfortunately, what we usually see on the market are all from foreign countries. The benefits taken away by foreigners in a year are incalculable. Therefore, several Cantonese merchants, such as Ma Ao, Xiao Guihong, Wang Zijia, Wang Yulin, Huang Qin, and others, specially raised capital in the 21st year of the Republic of China and established Huada Handkerchief Manufacturing Co., Ltd. in Jiuhefang, Hong Kong. The factory is equipped with new-style machines, specializing in the manufacture of various handkerchiefs, and has been registered by the governments of China, Britain, and the Philippines, with the Three Sheep brand as the trademark. The selection of raw materials and the promotion of business are all handled using scientific methods. Since the products are good, the sales are expanding day by day. It is now calculated that the places where they are sold are North China and South China in China, and the Nanyang Islands abroad. Although the goods are manufactured quickly, they are still not enough to distribute. Although the 21st year only operated for four months, the benefits obtained were not small.

Now, the advantages of the factory are briefly described for reference:

(1) Regarding organization and management: The factory has a general affairs department to take charge of everything, and also divides it into nine sections: business department, manufacturing, decoration, storage, design, publicity, accounting, receiving and dispatching, documents, and general affairs, to implement the spirit of division of labor and cooperation.

(2) Regarding products: The factory aims at modernization, such as the beauty of decoration, the novelty of patterns, etc., which are constantly being improved to meet the trend of the times.

(3) Regarding research and improvement: The factory stipulates that a meeting of staff members of each section is held every Saturday night, and everyone can express their opinions on how to improve the work, and the best ones are adopted.

(4) Regarding business: The factory uses new-style methods to attract customers and promote goods, so the three characters of the "Three Sheep Brand" have really been deeply imprinted in the minds of the Chinese people, and have long been recognized by people in the community.

The Efficacy of Golden Rooster Soap Essence, a National Product

In recent years, foreign goods have been dumped in large quantities, which has greatly affected our people's livelihood. Taking only the item of soap supplies as an example, how many millions of dollars are leaked every year? Looking at the root cause, most of it is because domestic soap products are either priced too high, or the efficacy is too low, or the smell is bad. Therefore, imported goods can run rampant. Now, industrial giants Liu Heqing, Xu Chunfan, and others have made a grand wish to hire chemical experts at a high price, collect various soap raw materials, and use scientific methods to research them dozens of times before inventing the Golden Rooster brand soap essence with amazing efficacy. It is said that all users who have used soap essence have unanimously praised it, saying that it has strong detergency, does not damage fabrics, sterilizes and disinfects, has a fragrant smell, is easy to use, does not require procedures, and is priced low, suitable for ordinary people, better than all soaps and soap powders, it is really good news in the year of national products.

A said, "National products are not as good as foreign goods."

A said, "Oh, I know. I will never buy foreign goods in the future. I will go to the China National Products Company to buy national products,..."

— Zhan Lu

His father especially approved of his son's concubinage plan, because his son's concubinage would give the old man hope of holding a grandson. Yang was from Qinzhou, Guangxi. Yang was an official in Guangzhou, and his father still lived in the countryside of Qinzhou. Blind Dance

— Yan Chonglou

Because of Hua's invitation, I stepped into the dance hall that I had not been to for a long time.

Although this dance hall is built in an open-air garden, it is shrouded in the atmosphere of the night. In the hall, only some black shadows can be seen flashing. The musicians play muddy tunes, plus the noisy voices of people. Although Hua tried his best to praise it as a summer resort, I knew that Hua said this to arouse my interest. In fact, this field not only cannot arouse my interest, but also adds some troubles to my troubled soul. We cannot endure long-term silence, so we subconsciously go to the field to dance.

In the darkness, I called a dancing girl from a seat. Maybe because of my illness and not dancing for a long time, my body seemed to be about to fall down. When I danced unnaturally with the dancing girl to a place with light, I suddenly caught a glimpse of the dancing girl's face. Huh! How could one of her eyes be blind? I was surprised! But my mood immediately returned to its original state. I remembered the blind prostitutes in Guangdong that were reported in the newspaper. They were bought when they were young, and when they grew up, the buyers blinded their eyes, so that they could arbitrarily sell their bodies without knowing the difference between black and white...

···This kind of story is prevalent in this tragic era. The one-eyed blind woman who is dancing with me now. And all the dancing girls whose eyes are not blind but are equal to blind, they are oppressed by life, they have no soul, no freedom, they are the most pitiful people in this world! This evil social system!··· I thought, my head seemed to explode, and at this moment the music suddenly stopped.

Hua and I returned to our original seats. Hua had just stumbled around with a short, fat dancing girl. I asked him how the dance was? He just smiled wryly. I felt that he was tasting the spiciness like me!

The music was still playing muddily, and the shadows were still flashing in the darkness. I didn't want to approach our blind dancing girl anymore, and I walked out of the dance hall surrounded by turbid air.

Northeast Fourth Company Commander

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter 12 Hardships of Military Service; A Sickly Man Falls Behind

Sacrifice and Disarmament; Soldiers are Sentimental

On this day, the night was still very long. Zhao Ziqiang walked to the window and saw that the sky was still silver-gray. The stars were sparse. Several bright stars as big as the mouth of a cup, like small light bulbs, were sinking down lonely in the air. The cold wind in the suburbs was even stronger in the morning. It was like scraping people's faces with a thin edge. Zhao Ziqiang looked at the sky, yawned twice in the cold, and thought in his heart that being a soldier was really too hard. Getting up so early, calling that young girl to marry a soldier.... Zhao Dequan, yes! Liu Jinsheng, yes! A rude, short burst of naming came from the cold. He thought again, I don't want to be dissatisfied anymore. As a company commander, I get up calmly, put on clothes and shoes, wash my face and gargle, too freely. But what about their soldiers? As soon as the bugle rang, the first one was the squad leader who jumped up. Within ten minutes, even the bed had to be cleaned up, and then he went to the yard to gather and stand in line, waiting for the roll call. In these ten minutes, I just walked from the front of the bed to the window. I didn't pat my leggings, and I didn't button the buttons under my clothes. They are all people, and this is enough to satisfy me. Thinking of this, his heart became happy, and he tidied up his clothes. It was seven o'clock, and it was time to drill. At this time, the stars in the sky were gone, but the sky was only slightly bright. The mist that had settled last night still enveloped the entire playground and had not been completely cleared. People from ordinary middle-class families who came out in such cold weather, in addition to their fur robes, even if they didn't wear an overcoat, would wrap a scarf around them. But what about the soldiers? They only wore a broken fur coat on their upper body and a pair of cotton trousers on their lower body. It didn't matter if most of the fur coats had lost their hair. The unbearable thing was the cotton trousers. The cotton wool inside was almost always re-fluffed old cotton wool. How could there be any warmth? (140)

Small Knowledge

Simple Stain Removal Method for Households

— Chu

Household daily necessities, contaminated with stains, should have considerable knowledge. Now, I will introduce several stain removal methods that I have personally tested:

Oils

Regardless of the various oils used for machinery, food, makeup, etc., the main component of the contamination is the non-drying oil quality mixed in the oil. To brush off the oil stains, first wash with soapy water, and then wipe with Vaseline, and the oil stains can naturally be removed. If it is silk clothes, which are not suitable for washing with soapy water, you can buy some deer horn cream or magnesium carbonate, apply it on the stain, cover it with a piece of absorbent paper, and press it with heavy objects. After about a day and night, the oil stain can be completely absorbed.

Ink

The ink contains pigments and iron. Oxalic acid must be used to remove iron, and then bleaching powder to remove pigments. If it has been a long time, ammonia water can be used to wash first, and then alcohol to wipe, and then soak in water to bleach.

Ink Juice

The ink also contains pigments. You can wash it with warm soapy water first, and then stick rice grains on the stain and put it into water to wash.

Blood

Blood contains protein and pigments. First wash off the pigments with warm soapy water, and then wipe with pinellia.

Fruit juice

Fruit juice contains sugar and acid. First use ammonia water to remove the acid, and then use warm water to wash away the sugar.

Rust

Rust only contains iron, which can be removed by washing with oxalic acid or acetic acid.

Paint

Paint contains drying oil and pigments. Wipe with sesame oil first, then wipe with volatile oil, and then wash with soapy water.

Summer Baths of Various Kinds

— Chu

In the summer, various ailments tend to occur, so in addition to paying attention to food and drink hygiene and residential hygiene every day, special attention should be paid to bathing. However, ordinary people only know how to use medicated water and soap, and do not know which medicine should be used to treat which disease. Now, I will introduce the most effective and proven Chinese herbal medicines:

Peach Leaf Water for Skin Diseases

Boil two or three liang of sun-dried peach leaves in boiling water until concentrated. Wash once or twice a day. This is very effective for dandruff, rashes, tinea, ringworm, athlete's foot, hemorrhoids, boils, etc. The water temperature should not be too cold when washing; the hotter, the better. First, use a cloth to filter out the peach leaf residue.

Sweet Flag Water for Nerve Pain

Sweet flag, which grows by the water, has roots that can be used as a tonic. It is very effective when decocted and taken internally by people with eye diseases. If you dry two or three plants of sweet flag, including the roots and leaves, add a handful of soap pods and four or five pieces of golden fist leaves, boil them together until concentrated, and use a cloth to filter the water. Wash once or twice a day. This is very effective for people with nerve pain and rheumatism.

Fennel Water During Pregnancy

Fennel seeds are often used by doctors as a stomach-strengthening and wind-dispelling medicine because they have a unique aroma. If you dry the leaves of fennel and boil them in water, it is very suitable for pregnant women and people who are sensitive to cold to bathe in it often. Moreover, the spirit is also refreshed because the nasal cavity and oral cavity are steamed with the aroma of fennel.

Angelica Water for Liver Pain

Angelica is the main medicine for women to replenish blood. It has a strong aroma. It is generally used for stomach diseases, liver qi diseases, gallstone pain, leucorrhea in women, etc. Use three or four qian of angelica, two or three qian each of Sichuan lovage, fennel, and cassia bark, add two bowls of water, boil them into a juice, and wash with it. It can relieve pain and dispel wind.

Hundred Herb Water for All Diseases

This is the leftover medicine scraps when pharmacists sort out various herbs. If you have skin diseases, women's diseases, gastrointestinal diseases, hemorrhoids, etc., it is very effective to wash with it.

Mulberry Leaf Water to Remove Dampness and Relieve Itching

Use dried mulberry leaves, winter mulberry leaves sold in pharmacies, add a piece of alum, huangbai, and two or three qian of sparse prickly ash. Boil them in water and wash with it. It can treat chronic eczema, remove dampness, relieve itching, kill bacteria, and disinfect. It is very effective.

Free Talk

More on "Pushing"

— Feng Zhiyu

After reading "The Pushing of the Third Kind of Person," I have some thoughts: Indeed, the work of "pushing" is now intensified, and the scope is also expanded. Thirty years ago, I often sat in the third-class cabin of Yangtze River steamships, but there was no such energetic "pushing" at that time.

At that time, you naturally had to buy a ticket, but there was no such thing as "buying a berth." There was buying at that time, but it was another matter. If you were afraid of not having a berth, you would go down to the ship with your luggage early in the morning. There were all empty berths in the third-class cabin, with only three or five people. But it was difficult to put your luggage down on an empty berth. Here a carrying pole, there a bundle of rope, here a roll of torn mat, there a vest. Someone would run out and say that the position was occupied by him. But at that time, you could have a meeting, advocate peace, and buy it from him. The highest value was generally eight jiao. If you were a fighting hero, it would be easy to deal with. Just sit nearby without saying a word. When the gong rang and the ship was about to leave, these territorialists would grab their carrying poles, torn mats, etc., and run away to the shore in a puff of smoke, leaving the unsold empty berths, allowing you to leisurely put your luggage down and go to sleep. If there were more people than berths and there was no way to accommodate them, we would sleep next to the berths. The "third kind of person" at the stern of the ship would not "push" you. Only the people resting outside the cabin doors had to go to the third-class cabin to avoid the purser when he checked tickets.

As for people who didn't buy tickets, they would undoubtedly be "pushed." The procedure was to confiscate their belongings, hang them on the mast or some pillar, pretending to beat them. But according to my eyewitness account, it was rare to actually beat them. When they reached the nearest pier, they would be "pushed" up. According to the stewards, they could also be "pushed" into the cargo hold and transported back to where they boarded the ship, but they didn't want to do this because "pushing" them to the nearest pier meant they had traveled one pier. "Pushing" them one by one, although they suffered some hardship, they eventually reached their destination.

The "third kind of person" in the past seemed to be more benevolent than now.

The pressure of life makes people烦冤, and in their confusion, they cannot see the冤家 clearly, so they think that family members and passers-by are obstructing their path, and therefore they "push." This is not only preserving oneself but also hating others. When this kind of person becomes wealthy, they want to "clear the way" when they come out.

I am not nostalgic for the past, but I am just saying that the work of "pushing" is now intensified and the scope is also expanded. I hope that future wealthy people will not "push" me to the "reactionary" pier, then I will be very fortunate.

An Elementary School Teacher's Opinion

— Shen Shiyuan

Ten years ago, I embraced the dream of "saving the country through education" and declined the assistance of relatives and friends. I did not go into business, nor did I engage in "acting on orders" tricks. I buried myself in elementary school education. At that time, I thought that education was a "sacred cause," but after two or three years, I realized that it was not so. In the eyes of local officials and gentry, elementary school teachers were almost equivalent to begging 化子.

However, I relied on some meager property and did not rely on a salary of ten or twenty yuan to support my family. Although the tuition was often in arrears, I still continued my blackboard and chalk life. I thought that as long as the teacher was enthusiastic and the students benefited, then even if people regarded me as a 化子, my career was still "sacred."

Until recently, I finally realized that I had completely failed. The biggest reason was that the textbooks I used seemed to be mocking my "ideal" in unison.

Let's take the Chinese textbook as an example. I have used the Chinese textbooks of several major bookstores. I remember often teaching such a story: Someone was poor when he was young, but he was diligent and thrifty, and later he became rich and lived a very comfortable life. It is extremely appropriate to teach people to be diligent and thrifty, but ending it with getting rich and living a comfortable life makes it seem that the only purpose of diligence and thrift is money. The impact on children's thinking is probably not good, right? And when I taught such a lesson, I felt like I was sitting on pins and needles, unable to feel at ease. Why? Because I am both diligent and thrifty, but I don't want to get rich. Instead, I can't get my salary, and I am willing to pay out of my own pocket because I believe that the purpose of life is greater than getting rich. If I am right, then why do the editors of the textbooks say that? I was very confused and indignant. Secondly, I am an honest person and I don't like being glib. Moreover, I have seen that the hangers-on in my relatives' families are all glib people, and I hate being glib. Unfortunately, I often encounter short stories of the "Xiaolin Guangji" type of glibness in textbooks. And children quickly learn this set. Eloquence may be one of the so-called "talents," but teaching young and innocent children to be glib like in the marketplace is probably not in line with the purpose of education, right? Why do the editors of textbooks like such teaching materials? This made me very puzzled again.

Furthermore, I am not against the stories of Cat Brother and Dog Brother. But I believe that children should not be reading only stories of Cat Brother and Dog Brother after their intelligence has developed to a certain stage. Unfortunately, some textbooks, all eight volumes, are all about Cat Brother and Dog Brother from beginning to end. However, the first few volumes are small cats and small dogs (that is, the stories are simple), and the last few volumes are cats and dogs with more complex minds. Whenever I teach these, I can't help but suspect that these textbooks are specially compiled for Cat Brother and Dog Brother to read.

I have always had these doubts, but I have never had a place to ask. Now that I see several gentlemen saying that they want to criticize textbooks and also hope that elementary school teachers will express their opinions, although I am no longer an elementary school teacher from this year, my opinion may be used as a reference, so I boldly wrote it out.

The Mistress and the Little Dog

— Xu Maoyong

When the National Crisis Conference opened last year, there was a comedy of demanding

the cancellation of party rule, and the result was that a certain gentleman's two crisp gongs and drums brought the scene to a leisurely conclusion: "There are only two ways to cancel party rule: first, the people automatically cancel it; second, the people revolt."

Now, some people have brought up the topic of "opening up political power," which is indeed much more moderate than "canceling party rule," so the same gentleman, without waiting for a popular revolt, has made remarks implying a willingness to open up.

But I think······ Oh! Writing to this point, I just realized that I have violated the forbidden regulations. The editor of Free Talk once advised people to "talk more about romance," how come I am talking about state affairs again? Damn it! Quickly change course, but I am not very "romantic," so let me tell a small story:

A mistress had a small key, which she used to open a small kitchen. In the kitchen was a small bottle, and in the bottle was a small piece of sugar. The mistress had a small dog, whose nature was very playful. It liked to grab the mistress's skirt and pull it.

The mistress took the small key and opened her small kitchen, taking out a small piece of sugar from the small bottle. The little dog looked up and wagged its tail. The mistress said: "Gaprisa Petrovna, you pull my skirt, now look at this piece of sugar, but you must not eat it."

The mistress put the piece of sugar back in its original place. The little dog regretted it, but it was too late. (From page 177 of the Collection of Foreign Novels)

The author of this story, Sologub, is a Russian novelist, not a Chinese satirist. This should be stated.

I Also Talk About the So-Called "Four Treasures Series"

— Wu Jiu

The opinions expressed by Mr. Wang He in Free Talk a few days ago regarding the so-called "Four Treasures Series" are very insightful, but his vision is somewhat limited to the cultural circle, and he has not noticed that the "Four Treasures Series" will be a commodity, and what he does not approve of from a cultural standpoint is actually the key to making a fortune in the future with a tenfold profit, which is somewhat lacking.

In my opinion, the bookstore's photolithographic "Four Treasures Series" is entirely "commercial in nature." Everything is determined by this "commercial nature." If you understand this nature, then what Mr. Wang He thinks is incompatible with the cultural nature can be understood in its consistency and mystery, and his high proposal to publicly select items and have scholars discuss and decide can no longer be hoped for.

For example, Mr. Wang He believes that it is somewhat insulting to contemporary scholars to have someone like Jiang Fusong, the director of the preparatory office of the Central Library, who has no common sense, select the catalog of the so-called "Four Treasures Series." But from a commercial point of view, the so-called scholars are not as capable of rallying people as the director of the preparatory office of the Central Library. Also, Mr. Wang He believes that book collectors may not have scholarship and should not ask their opinions, but should ask the opinions of scholars. But from a commercial point of view, it is not as good as asking the opinions of book collectors, because asking their opinions is tantamount to asking major customers. As for the so-called impoverished scholars, Mr. Wang He may think they are valuable, but in the eyes of businessmen, they are not worth a penny, and they will not pay a high price to buy books for collection. Furthermore, regarding the so-called "communication of international culture," Mr. Wang He seems to think it is too exaggerated, but from a commercial point of view, it should be exaggerated to be an advertisement. And if we deduce from a commercial perspective, we can also deduce what the so-called "Four Treasures Series" will be.

It will be like this: printed exquisitely, so book collectors will love it; sold at a very high price, so book collectors can boast that only a few of them have it in their collections, and the general public cannot see it; therefore, it must not be sold separately, so as to satisfy the unique interest of book collectors.

As for us poor kids who want to read books, we still have to honestly go to the library that houses the "Complete Library of the Four Treasuries" to copy it, just like now.

Ordinary Things (24)

— 𣽃 Guosun

The team leader meant that although Zhiguang's goal was to go to Zhazha Changxing, the mud workers were not completely staying at the Liu family's house, and maybe they were scattered from north of the Liu family's house all the way to Jiangwan Yanghang, so why did he have to go to the Liu family's house? If he took the small road from here to Dachang, and then walked eastward from Dachang towards Jiangwan, the danger would be reduced. It was only dangerous when crossing Zhongshan Road. Moreover, when he got there, it might already be dark without needing a mirror at all. When it was dark, it would be extra safe.

So Zhiguang accepted the team leader's opinion and decided to wait until after three o'clock before setting off, so that he would arrive at Dachang just in time for darkness.

However, in less than half an hour, a new situation unfolded: the foreman of Chenjia浜 received an order from the team leader: "Make rice at four o'clock, check all the completed materials at five o'clock, and prepare to set off with the whole team." And Zhiguang himself also received a letter from the team leader, who advised him not to go north today, and not to go east either. It would be better to wait until tomorrow to see the situation, because the situation was particularly serious, and the army was building fortifications on the north-east side all night long······ Finally, he also mentioned "the difficulty of transportation."

The so-called "whole team" meant that even those who were not on the night shift had to work. Of course, the situation suddenly became tense, presumably because there would be a fierce battle that night. So Zhiguang also suddenly felt new difficulties. He thought that if he didn't go to see those mud workers, he would feel very uneasy in his heart. If he went to see them, he would have to wait another whole day. However, he would delay the matter of providing assistance for at least another day! Finally, after many deliberations, he decided, according to the representatives' suggestion, to rush back to Shanghai immediately with them to find Yao Botang and try to make the assistance a reality quickly and sufficiently.

Their return journey was by the small road southwest of Chenjia浜, diagonally across the railway, and then into Zhongshan Road. They then walked carefully and cautiously south on Zhongshan Road for three or four li to reach the southern embankment of the New Dachang Bridge in Caojiadu. At this time, the Italian soldiers guarding the concession checkpoint were single-mindedly waiting for the order from their commander to close the checkpoint amid the yellow错. Zhiguang said sadly to the representatives:

"In the concession, we may be the last people to break into the New Dachang Bridge today!"

After four o'clock this day, Yao Botang had summarized the opinions of various companies in the same industry regarding the assistance to Zhabei into a conclusion, which was: "Temporarily perfunctory, and slowly deal with it." In other words, whether supporting or opposing, both were canceling the extreme attitude. Originally, these Alash-style people, with their big bellies and old faces, speaking glibly, almost always held this kind of attitude regarding all issues concerning the future of the nation. However, Botang was not entirely like this. In terms of his temperament, he was originally a descendant of a noble family who had not forgotten propriety and righteousness. In terms of his knowledge, he was indeed an engineer who understood the times. In terms of his assets, he was also a "bourgeois" who was half-declined and eager to revive. The combination of these three atoms created the new-style entrepreneur Yao Botang that we see in reality. Of course, he had always been unwilling to completely agree with the opinions of the general Alash-style entrepreneurs in Shanghai, especially since this time the assistance to Zhabei was related to both personal wealth and the nation! In Botang's consciousness, personal wealth certainly occupied an important position, but he was also unwilling to abandon the nation. Unfortunately, the interests of these two aspects often conflicted with each other, so when he understood from the conclusion that the negative proposals of his colleagues were too unwise, he held a belly full of considerations to find a way to reconcile the contradictions in his heart and plan a wise proposal. This was truly worth considering! However, without receiving the representatives' specific conditions, all kinds of proposals were inevitably aimed at nothing, so in the end, he had only one way to wait quietly.

When the progress lights were just on, Zhiguang led the three representatives. These three representatives first mentioned their initial hopes to Botang, then described the situation they had experienced in Zhabei that day, and then stated that they thought assistance trucks were better than anything else, so they hoped that the factory would provide as many trucks as possible. Business Economics (24)

Winter Mushrooms' Sister: Straw Mushrooms

Straw mushrooms and fragrant winter mushrooms are both plants of the genus . But unlike fragrant winter mushrooms, they can be planted anywhere. The shapes are also different. Straw mushrooms are white in color, and the umbrella is thicker and smaller, and the stem is fat and thick, and there is no fragrant gas. But the taste is absolutely delicious compared to fragrant winter mushrooms, even better than them.

Straw mushrooms are produced in the northeast of a few provinces, of which Jilin products are the best. Among the Jilin goods, the ones produced near the ancient pagoda are the highest in body. Duolun, Inner Mongolia's Lama Temple is also good, the Eight Banners goods are second, and the outer Eight Banners produce the next. The levels of the goods are roughly divided. (1) The temple is large and self-generated, each one is selected, the color is bright and clean: the quality is 2 fat and thick. (2) 裏 Large Self-Generated: The color is bright: the shape is uniform. (3) Large Self-Generated; is the goods of the Outer Eight Banners, the next. (4) Jingkou Ding; (5) Beikou, large self-generated and below, the goods are inferior in body, the color is dim and black, and the shape is uneven. Therefore, the advantages of the best straw mushrooms are (1) the color is bright and pure; (2) the shape is round and neat; (3) the volume is plump and thick; (4)

Identity is dry. Otherwise, it is the so-called substandard goods

Straw mushrooms are loaded in grass bags from the place of origin. They are carried by camels to Zhangjiakou and concentrated; then in Zhangjiakou, they are repackaged in wooden boxes and strictly

Sealed and transported to various places for sale. The wooden box is square, and each box weighs about 40-50 pounds.

Straw mushrooms are the only treasure in vegetarian food, of course, the sales volume of temples and vegetarian restaurants is the largest. The most powerful people who transship from Shanghai for export are the Sichuan merchants, because the output is not large, but the demand is eager. So it feels quite valuable. At present, the market price per load is about 700 yuan for the top grade and 300-400 yuan for the middle grade. When it was most expensive one or two years ago, it sold for more than 1,300 yuan. This is inevitably a bit aristocratic. Straw mushrooms are a special product of our country. (Japan has none, France has military straw

Mushrooms, only have canned), but since the September 18th Incident, half of the northeast has fallen to foreign countries, what do people in the country think when they taste this delicious food!

Talk

On Women

— Wu

Some people say: Women are just things for men to look at. Suddenly, it seems that the words are too excessive, and there is a suspicion of insulting women, but after careful taste, it is not a deceptive statement. For example, the Chinese use flowers to describe women, and Westerners use birds to describe women. When it comes to description, it should be the matter of literary figures, such as Li Taibai's "Hibiscus is like a face and willow is like eyebrows" and Ibsen's "My little pine"

Rats", are all the same in different ways, describing Yang Guifei and Nora as very cute. However, what kind of "thing" are women in the eyes of men? It is already said clearly here, do you need to argue strongly?

To tell you the truth, since the era of the matrilineal society, women have been nothing more than flowers in the pot and birds in the cage of men. It was so in the era of handicrafts, and even more so in the era of mechanical industry. The only reason is that their productivity is weak, and the relationship of childbearing, so men take advantage of their weaknesses, enslave them, use them, and all life is taught to them to be given to men. "At home, follow the father, when married, follow the husband, and when the husband dies, follow the son", aren't these the definitions that stipulate that they are appendages of men? So they have to obey him, obey him, serve him, be considerate of him, comfort him, love him, love him, flatter him, and use their lips to caress him, and use their thighs to satisfy him, to pass on his lineage, and to educate his children for him. Therefore, they have to have a charming face. Therefore, they have food to eat and clothes to wear in life, and coffins and coffins in death. It turns out that women are such "things". In addition, the private social system has pressed her into various forms, so that they have the distinction of wives, teachers, Misses, girls, mother-in-law, elder sister, female workers, and prostitutes. They are private property, and they are also commodities. Especially in this year of national crisis, women are even more in the autumn of misfortune. Many people blame women for loving luxury and not being thrifty. The biggest accusation is that they are unwilling to patronize domestic products. As a certain old writer said; "As if women had entered the monastery, the national crisis would be saved." This is just as the history of the past dynasties has recorded, almost every time the country was destroyed, it was related to the beautiful women who were obsessed with the country and the city. Even "falling horse buns" and "sad eyebrows" are signs of the destruction of the country. In fact, it is not that the world will prosper without beautiful women, although every traitor or dying doctor cannot help but regard beautiful women as important as tens of millions of family wealth, but there are not many heroes who did not marry oriental beauties and use the four northeastern provinces as dowries. As for the gentlemen who scold women as "vampires"

"The family of destruction" puts on a stern face to maintain morality, and even scolds them for not being willing to buy two pairs of Chinese silk stockings a day. But they secretly admire women's thighs under the dim light, and the irrepressible lust caused by their foreign gauze and silk cover-ups is not also a vicious manifestation of this class of orthodox gentlemen and domestic product gentlemen? However, it is only that women who have been raised by men cannot help but let them scold them. In fact, this is exactly their pity.

The above said a lot, maybe another typical man will scold me for bowing down to the pomegranate skirt and willingly defending women. However, I ask myself that my proposition is extremely fair. In fact, if there are really no prostitutes who buy prostitutes in the current society, there will never be prostitutes who sell prostitutes. From wife to maid, they all exist for men's enjoyment, and the reason why they are so distressed is that private economy buried them in the fire pit. Then how can the enlightened and brave female comrades save themselves? In addition to actively seeking the creation of a new world, there is probably no other way.
