(Yet rewarded)

Life is Green Mountains Everywhere!

— Xue An

This happened two years ago. But the impression of this event is still deeply etched in my mind. The fact is this:

In the factory where I worked, there was a lack of specialized technical talent in mechanical engineering at the time. Later, a young Japanese worker was introduced by a technician. He was visiting China for the first time, and he often showed a surprised and astonished attitude towards Chinese customs and habits. After finishing his work, he often stood alone, as if pondering something.

"He is wandering alone in China. During his spare time, he must be missing his hometown," I thought.

"Friend, the pressure of the environment is really terrible. You left your lovely hometown for the sake of bread and came to a strange foreign country to find work. In your spare time, do you feel the dryness and loneliness of life in a foreign country and miss your hometown?" I asked him.

After hearing my words, he didn't answer me, just smiled slightly; he took out a pencil from his work clothes pocket and wrote twenty-eight characters on a piece of paper:

"A man should set his ambitions and leave his hometown, and never return until he achieves something. Why bury his bones in his hometown? Life is green mountains everywhere."

"Life is green mountains everywhere!" What a thought-provoking line of poetry.

Among us Chinese, who are full of strong hometown concepts, except for a few provinces along the coast, it seems that it is rare for people to go to other places to investigate or seek development in life. Some of them rely on the legacy of their ancestors and do the work of "guarding the family property" in their hometowns; others, although they have no fixed property and live a mediocre life in their hometowns, are also "safe in poverty" because of the saying "It's good to be at home for a thousand days, but difficult to go out for one day." Most people generally live with the idea of ​​spending their lives in their hometowns, and they are reluctant to leave their hometowns easily unless there is something unavoidable.

When others organize investigation teams and explorers, enduring hardship, to investigate and explore our land, we, who have always adhered to the principle of苟安(苟安: content with the present situation), of course have no interest in doing this kind of "foolish" work. Others have investigated our mineral, agricultural products, customs and habits in great detail, and we, who are kept in the dark, of course don't know. (And it is "beneath our dignity to know" - evolving from "beneath our dignity to do"). Others use force to rob our resources. That doesn't matter either, these things have nothing to do with us directly, so let them rob them! Fortunately, we have the timeless lessons of "protecting oneself wisely" and "everyone sweeps the snow from their own door"!

If we don't want to do anything, then so be it. If we want to revitalize our own country, on the one hand

Page 20

it is necessary to reform the social system and put politics on track; on the other hand, we must first examine ourselves and reform our minds, which have been nurtured by precious teachings.

On the Singlehood Society that Upholds Ambition

— Pei Shan

Reading the newspaper, I saw that in High Wycombe, Buckinghamshire, England, more than a hundred young people organized a bachelor club, which was spread as a novel event. It should be known that young people organizing singlehood groups, Chinese youth, had precedents long ago. Three years ago, students of Jiangwan Chizhi University already had an organization of a singlehood society. The reporter was also one of the founders that day. At that time, more than two hundred students participated, which can be said to be a great event for a time. The name of this society is called the Singlehood Society in Chinese, and BachelorClub in English. The society organization has a president, directors, clerks, accountants, investigation and other sections: all of which are produced by the general election. The work in the society is the busiest in the investigation section, because the section is responsible for investigating whether the members joining the society are 광夫(a bachelor). If it is found that they are married or have lovers, they must be expelled from the society according to the regulations and must be punished. The society is getting deeper and deeper. Young men should devote themselves to the country and should not marry and have children and live a sweet sexual life, because once a young person has a wife, he will become listless and prematurely senile. At the same time, morbid conditions such as corruption and decadence will also arise from this, and they will only know that they have a family and not a country, so they advocate a singlehood society so that ambitious young people can concentrate on saving the country without the burden of a wife. (2) Because the level of life is getting higher and higher, the youth economy cannot be independent, and it is not easy to make a living. It is not enough to support oneself. Moreover, modern women are vain and live extravagantly, and it is not easy to support them. Furthermore, under the feudal Chinese old family system, young people's marriage is not free and are subject to various family constraints, all of which are the main reasons for inciting young people to advocate singlehood. It is also the original reason why we organized the singlehood society that day, which was completely motivated by the times and social background.

Most of the main members of our singlehood society that day were third- and fourth-year college students. They were busy with their studies, so after its establishment, the society's affairs gradually became sluggish. Even members broke their vows and got married and pursued girls outside the school. Therefore, they were attacked by students outside the society, saying that the members of our society were all organizations that regretted women after being lovelorn, and that if all Chinese young people did not get married, they would create small citizens, and they were afraid that they would become extinct in the future, and there would be no descendants to avenge the country. This is a serious national issue. They also said that we are all sinners of the nation, etc. Because of this society, I had a lot of written lawsuits with my classmates on the school's bulletin board that day, and as a result, both sides wasted a lot of precious time! Later, our singlehood society also disappeared invisibly with our golden age school life! Some of the members of the singlehood society that day are now married and have children! And some are still single. The singlehood society, which was so prosperous for a time, has only left a youthful dream, which is always memorable.

Finally, I would like to introduce a few famous sayings from Professor Xia Jinlin of our alma mater, which served as the closing statement of the singlehood society that day: "Young men and women! If you think it is good to get married, then go get married. If you think it is good to be single, then be determined to be single. Follow your personal philosophy of life, not your curiosity and the ideas you get from academic theories."

Twenty-Two of Modern Celebrities' Paintings and Calligraphy

Mr. Ying Yeping's Painting (Brief Biography)

Ying Jun, styled Yeping, is from Ninghai, Zhejiang. He inherited his family learning at a young age and had already mastered the essentials of the Six Principles of Painting. After arriving in Shanghai, he studied with Zheng Wuchang, a famous figure in the art world, and his skills improved further. He learned figure painting from Chen Hongshou, who was ancient, vigorous, and elegant, yet clear and free and easy. His landscape painting started with Shitao and Qushan, and he obtained the mantle of his teacher, 清輕淡宕(Qīng qīng dàn dàng: light and unrestrained).

Reminiscences

— Wu

This is still last year's fact

My friend Mr. Liu and I walked out of the cinema, it was already half past eleven at night. The heat of the day had not completely dissipated due to the night air, but the cool breeze was pleasant. Our footsteps were particularly heavy in the empty streets. Most of the colorful electric lights had been turned off, only Tearooms or Cafes were still open, waiting for the last batch of "mysterious" people unique to this "mysterious street." At this time, I mustered up my courage and said to Mr. Liu

"Let's go, let's go to that Cafe for a drink"

"Let's have ice cream, I'm terribly thirsty."

"I agree," Mr. Liu immediately responded, "but we have to go to a store with female waitresses, in order to know what the so-called young and beautiful female waitresses are all about."

So we stepped into the "White Russian" store.

As soon as we entered the door, those white-clothed "waiters" shouted "Guests!" and escorted us up the stairs, followed by giggling girls who led us into a "refined" room, followed by moving the screen and lowering the curtains, "Okay, now we finally got them." But I was worried, I had to carefully calculate my money, but it wasn't enough, I had to ask Mr. Liu in Japanese with a beating heart:

I said a sentence in Japanese, meaning "Do you have a lot of money?"

He said "Yes," so I was relieved, but I saw the "female waitress" sitting on Mr. Liu's body giggle at me for a while, followed by coyly saying:

(It doesn't matter, aren't you all rich?)

"Oh? You understand Japanese?" Mr. Liu was simply shocked, and my face couldn't help but be covered with a burst of heat: "Ah, she has broken our secret." So, in their soft and charming laughter, the girl who spoke Japanese bluntly made the decisions for us. We each had a ham and egg, and she herself wanted to eat a加次萊司(Japanese Curry Rice), in addition to half a dozen beers and a bottle of wine, of course, this was also for herself. So from then on it was eating, drinking, talking, laughing Shanghai dialect, Jiangbei dialect, Japanese, pidgin English, hugging, kissing, and cigarettes, cigars. Three hours later, we walked out of the store, Mr. Liu wiped his forehead and said to me:

"Ah! So this is the female waitress in Shanghai,"

I knew it.

This year's summer night, the "mysterious street" is naturally very different. But how much has it changed? I don't know, and my friend Mr. Liu will never know.

Employee Correspondence

Marriage and Economic Problems

Editor:

I am now years old, a junior clerk in a foreign company, with a monthly income of more than twenty yuan, which must be deducted for car and other expenses, leaving very little. Sent home for family use. My father also works in a foreign company, with no property, and his income is enough to support himself. Several years ago, my family wanted to get me married. Because I knew that my academic ability was insufficient, I intended to study, so I refused. And I once said, "If I don't have the ability to be independent, I will never get married!" My family couldn't help it. Now that my mother has passed away, and no one is taking care of the family affairs, my father is eager to get me married, and replied to me: "Father can definitely find you a better job."

So my marriage can no longer be postponed. A few days ago, I even preliminarily engaged with a neighbor's daughter, and the wedding date is not far away. The required expenses were somehow made up, and now I am just waiting for the wedding date to arrive. But I worry that my old father is getting older and weaker, and I expect that he will not be able to help me for a long time. If I am unlucky in the future, and my business is still not developing as before, and it is difficult to continue my ambitions, and the expenses will increase in the future, and I will not be able to repay the debt, then the future environment is quite worrying. Furthermore, I am currently borrowing money to get married, and I have said before: "If I am not independent, I will never get married." Will this cause any loss of reputation to me? Will I be laughed at? Besides this, is there a better plan? Please don't mind the trouble, and answer in detail. I am very grateful! Sincerely, Huang Juefei

Answer: "If I don't have the ability to be independent, I will never get married," this is a slogan of modern youth. At first glance, it is not beautiful and pleasant to hear, but upon careful study, we can find its contradictions and inconsistencies. "Marriage" is originally a very natural thing. As long as the two sexes love each other, they can get together at any time. Now why should an irrelevant condition be added: "If I cannot be independent, I will never..."? Generally speaking, the surface reasons are: First, women's economy cannot be independent and must rely on men. If men's economic ability cannot be independent, then this family is extremely dangerous; Second, women's economy cannot be independent, and men's livelihoods are also very difficult. If men cannot get a reliable and permanent job that is sufficient to be independent, and rashly get married, their future will naturally be very dangerous. Therefore, due to these two reasons, it is advocated that men cannot marry without the ability to be independent. However, I want to ask further: Why can't women be independent? Why is the problem of men's livelihoods so difficult? If in another system society, the private ownership system does not exist, and no one has the idea of gains and losses and greed, and men and women all have considerable work to do, and can maintain a general life that is not much different, may I ask: When men and women in this society combine with each other, do they have to ask whether the man can be independent, and then add the condition "If I cannot be independent, I will never..."? Of course they don't! Absolutely not! Because their men and women can be independent in life, no one relies on anyone, and no one will have the panic of unemployment. They naturally don't need this kind of economic condition to prevent the family from breaking down due to economic problems in advance! So, after all is said and done, this problem is superficially a marriage problem, but in essence, it still belongs to the entire social problem. Since this problem is the entire social problem, we can only solve it fundamentally. If we don't get married because of economic difficulties, is this expressing submission to the oppression of society? The rich can have three wives and four concubines, why can't we poor people marry one wife? So you say that because of economic difficulties, you won't get married, this is a passive method, equivalent to giving up eating because of choking. And even if you don't get married, you still can't solve our poverty! We must solve our poverty by fundamental methods. It is completely wrong to use not getting married as a passive resistance!

For example: you say that you will never get married if you are not economically independent, then I have to ask you: When will your economic problems be independent? If you go to be a running dog of the oppressive class, and fatten yourself by dipping into their leftovers, or use other illegal methods to earn some property, you can solve this problem. If you do business step by step, no matter how diligent and thrifty you are, you will not be able to be economically independent in a hundred years! Not only can you not be independent, but judging from the current situation, if there is no change in this society, I am afraid that your life will only get worse day by day, and you will eventually end up with nothing. I ask you: Are you waiting for the society to change before you get married? This is of course an untenable argument.

Therefore, I think that the "marriage" problem, if you think it is necessary, you might as well "marry." As for the life problem, you should think about it from a larger perspective and seek a fundamental solution. And this solution is definitely not something that can be solved by being diligent and thrifty and finding a good job. This is just a way to treat the head when it hurts and the foot when it hurts. The so-

called fundamental solution is to start from the root of the problem. Of course, I am not saying that you don't need to be diligent and thrifty and strive to learn. It is very necessary.

Finally, the letter said that my father has raised a thousand yuan. Judging from your economic situation, this amount does not seem to be used. I think everything can be saved. Except for the necessary expenses, any unrealistic pomp should be abolished. The union of men and women is originally normal. The so-called lifelong events are all lies that feudal society uses to deceive people. Don't believe them. You should be casual and casual.

Finally, you said that borrowing money to "get married" will be ridiculed? What does it matter? If you think you are doing the right thing, why bother if others ridicule you? What is reputation or disgrace is also a lie! If you are so hungry that you have to rob something to eat, see if you still want reputation? One more thing to add, your letter seems to have a feeling of regret that you cannot rely on your father to enjoy a long and happy life. This kind of decadent consciousness is also absolutely undesirable!

Correction: In the third line from the end of yesterday's draft, the "求和二字係" (the two words "seek peace") is a mistake for "示知" (to inform). I hereby correct it.

He was immediately diagnosed and treated. He was quickly cured. After that, he was lively and fat. He was safe and sound. Unexpectedly, in the recent month, his head suddenly became swollen. (The skin all around is soft) It is increasing day by day. Compared with the face from the ears, nose, and below, it has almost doubled. His body is getting weaker day by day. The pupils of both eyes are often sluggish downwards. His neck is raised with great effort. His diet is normal. His urination is smooth. Only his bowel movements are sparse. Novel

Under the Traffic Lights (37)

— Xi Lin

He helplessly walked back and forth on the side of the Malley Hotel. This was not to stalk the third concubine, but to pass the painful time. However, it was ineffective. The more he walked back and forth, the more anxious he became like an ant spinning in a hot pot. So he decided to go back into the hotel and shamelessly ask the tea room staff

The tea room staff, who are the best at finding out secrets, had already seen through his heart from Shi Qiao's actions. Shi Qiao had only made a gesture. One of them had already gotten up to tell him that the third concubine had looked at the room and gone out again. The gentleman who came with her was short, fat, and very happy! I don't know when they will be back. If Shi Qiao wants them to tell him the room number, just give them some benefits. He can open a room next door to the third concubine's room. Shi Qiao agreed to all their conditions. He sat there dumbfounded in the next room. Now his curiosity has exceeded his jealousy. Who is that short, fat, and happy person?

Soon, someone suddenly pushed open the door as if they were walking into their own room. Shi Qiao poked his head out to see that it was none other than Wang Hua. Wang Hua obviously looked a little embarrassed. He went to the wrong room. He couldn't help but laugh dryly a few times first, then stepped forward and held Shi Qiao's hand, holding it tighter than usual. He said;

"Shi Qiao, haha, I actually ran into you! Great! I have something to discuss with you! Ha, ha, ha!"

"Ha, ha, ha, great! Shi Qiao laughed forcefully. He fixed his mind and looked at Wang Hua's body all over. Short, fat, and very happy. Great, ha, ha, ha!

Wang Hua has always been an optimist. He never sticks to things or takes them seriously. When he learned that Shi Qiao had exposed his secrets, he was also straightforward, but he said nonchalantly:

"You are writing a detective novel of love! Shi Qiao, Mrs. Yang is Mrs. Yang after all. Anyway, she is someone else's! I think she is better to you!"

In this way, Shi Qiao's anger was not easy to vent. But without Wang Hua's consent, he pushed open the door and walked to the next door. Wang Hua followed behind with a smile. He said!

"She hasn't come back yet? Maybe she won't come back. I'm not the only one accompanying her tonight. Shi Qiao, we are all being led around by her!"

Shi Qiao saw that there was indeed no one in the room. At first, he felt a little relieved. As long as Wang Dwarf is also waiting in vain tonight, that's enough to make him feel a little comfortable. Later, when he thought of Wang Dwarf saying that he was not the only one accompanying her tonight, he felt that all his jealousy and anger were superfluous. But he, who has always been serious about doing things, could not help but feel

Film Special Issue

The Metamorphosis of Future Films

— Guang Dao

Predictions of the Development of Wireless Films

It is Not Impossible for Every Household to Own One

The things that will be stored away in the future and waiting for us to discover are truly ever-changing and elusive. However, this wireless film "Television," a mixture of radio and film, is already not far from us. Some say that by 1940, we will be able to have one in every household, sitting in the living room and turning the dial on the machine to watch sound films on the wall or a small screen. On the one hand, we are amazed at the omnipotence of science, and on the other hand, we are ashamed of our lack of inventive genius, and can only sit at home and enjoy the fruits of it.

From watching silent films to watching sound films, from playing phonographs to playing radios, we have already felt that a new century has been created in the past ten years or so. If wireless film succeeds in the future, wouldn't we be entering a new era again? According to scientists, the future wireless film machine will be roughly the same as the current radio, but there will be an extra screen in the house. When the show starts, just turn the dial on the machine, the sound will come out of the machine, and the image will appear on the screen. At the same time, it can be like the current radio, and you can freely pick up any wireless film station's broadcasts by controlling the length of the radio waves. According to David Sarnoff of RCA, in the future, every family can have a small theater, and we can watch plays, boxing matches, horse races, football, or listen to concerts at will.

This wireless film is not a new invention. Although it is still in the inventor's laboratory, it is gradually being completed and improved, and will soon be available for practical use. It is said that it is now possible to see some scenery transmitted nearby in two small telescopes, and the sound is quite accurate. In the future, if the range of scenery to be transmitted is expanded and the sound transmission machine is perfected, it can be made public to the world.

As for the future method of wireless film broadcasting, there are probably only two types. The simplest is the broadcast of sound films. When wireless film is completed in the future, broadcasting movies will not be a problem. This method is to collect important news from all over the world, create films, and when they are shown in cinemas, they can be broadcast to homes using television. Of course, all ordinary films can be broadcast by television. And this broadcasting method can be used to unite all cinemas to establish a central broadcasting station: the film is transmitted from the central station to each cinema. In this way, one film copy can be enough for hundreds of cinemas. The second method is to have special personnel collect the scenery from the place where an event occurs and broadcast it directly to cities, cinemas, and private homes all over the world. This is exactly the same as broadcasting a speech in a large gathering now.

After this news came out, many theater and cinema owners became worried. They are afraid that in the future, everyone will use a wireless film machine (Televisor) at home to play movies themselves, and there will be no need to go to the theater. But many people believe that a large number of people still like to go to cinemas and do not want to sit at home and play movies themselves. Ordinary people are used to staying at home and find it boring: they can meet many friends, see many people, and feel more comfortable in theaters or cinemas. The air in the theater is completely different from the air at home. After all, sitting at home can only see a part of what is broadcast, and everything around the theater cannot be seen. In this way, they still have to come out. On this point, I also feel that some people like to sit at home, of course they still sit at home; and those who can't sit still at home still have to come out. Otherwise, there are many people now who have phonographs and radios at home, but they still have to come out to play. Will they not come out in the future when they have wireless film machines?

Film Review

Review of "A Woman of New York" Mandon Broadway

— Ling He

If We Have to Estimate the Existence Value of This Film

, then the performance of the male lead Robert Montgomery, in that light and lively mood, is very worthy of people's attention. His lively movements and quick expressions are difficult to find in other young American male actors. I remember that it seemed that a newspaper once praised him as the most popular young actor in the United States. His acting skills can indeed cater to the happy mood of noble audiences. His bright movements and dialogues can be used as recall material for them after tea and dinner. Therefore, Montgomery is after all a lovable child.

In addition, the name Sally Eilers cannot be ignored. Especially her collaboration with Gibson in "Good Luck" showed her success in acting. But the role she played here is not very brilliant, perhaps the plot limited her development, compared with the role of the small jasper she played before, she did not surpass her previous achievements after all. However, when she explained the murder process in front of the plainclothes police, she still showed her skillful technique.

But besides acting, what other achievements can we find? I dare not compliment, it is precisely the emptiness of the content that determines the mediocrity of the performance. I don't understand why the author of this film wants to make a protagonist the focus of the play, but the result is that Montgomery is singing a solo in a plot that is empty and without anything. At the same time, we know that the author's original intention is only to give the audience a light and refreshing summer reliever, but the form of comedy is not necessarily always easy. The smooth mood certainly cannot be as touching and profound as that of a tragedy, but good comedies are not completely unable to make people remember for a long time. Therefore, I think the biggest lack of this film is not paying attention to the ups and downs of the mood, like a white cardboard, it cannot make me feel personally. This comedy is of course overshadowed in all aspects compared with "Millions" or "The Flowing Years," and it is also not as good as the "Good Luck" mentioned earlier. Even in terms of Montage, although it is not too cumbersome, it is not economical. For example, the virtuous wife is written very insufficiently, especially the reunion on the ship should not have accidental tricks. As for saying that this divorced couple still loves each other, then we can't see it on the book besides the instructions.

However, in terms of content, if you don't care about its vulgar and boring shortcomings, then you can still find some unexpected gains. For example, the officials below the mayor actually discuss political issues in nightclubs, and the sociable nightclub owners can use their ability to reverse the situation, bribe and plead for favors, and use despicable methods to acquit murderers, which can all explain the darkness of politics and the deception of the law. Regarding these, the gentlemen who care about the world and the hearts of the people sigh

Audience Opinions

Talking About "Eternal Regret"

— Yi Ju

After watching "Eternal Regret," people feel that the products of Chinese small film companies have not yet embarked on the right path, which is very disappointing.

The opening explanation of "Eternal Regret" said that the purpose of this film is to promote science, (the general meaning is indeed so) but the plot performance is absurd and outrageous, and I don't know where the so-called "promoting science" starts? In this film, I only saw a few cars coming and going from time to time, and a few scenes of funny and ridiculous fights. I sat silently for two hours and walked out, feeling infinitely disappointed

There are many inappropriate things in the plot performance of "Eternal Regret": (1) The love life and separation of Yu Qing and Li Lian are performed from Li Lian's memories, which is not sufficient, (2) Yu Qing quarreled with the servants because of playing the piano, and even started fighting. Is this the true color of young people? Yu Qing is not a strong man, but he can fight against five or six people, who would believe it? (3) The theft of the pearl chain in Yu Qing's house is not so easy. How the thief entered the house is not shown. (4) Li Lian did not know that the old man was Zhi Qi's disguise, but she dared to boldly follow him and sneak into the secret room. Judging from the performance on the money screen, Li Lian is definitely not this kind of woman. (5) Zhi Qi started a conflict because Li Lian saw through the secret, and Yu Qing walked over and saw it, and even went up to fight with Zhi Qi. This is too unreasonable. What right does Yu Qing have to interfere with them? Yu Qing is not a chivalrous man. (6) Writing about Zhi Qi's invention of an airplane that can exceed the speed of ordinary airplanes by three times, and Guanghui's invention of missiles, did not explain the principle, making the audience feel inexplicable

Miss Hu Die Touched by the Scene

Rain also has a sense of past and present

The weather was terribly hot the other day. Coincidentally, "Spring Silkworms" was filming a rainy scene. On the photography scene, the fire hydrant was turned on, and artificial rain was falling heavily. For a while, water splashed and flew all over the sky, and the heat was dissipated. Director Cheng Bugao took off his shoes and socks and directed the work, his thighs covered with mud. Hu Die stood by and watched, and saw Gao Qianping and Wang Zhengxin walking back and forth in the rain to act. She remembered the situation when she was filming "Mad Current" last winter. At that time, the weather was severely cold, and everyone was shaking from being hit by this violent artificial rain. Touched by the scene, she couldn't help but sigh: Miss Gao and the others are really enjoying themselves, taking a shower on such a hot day: We were filming "Mad Current" last year, how could we be so comfortable!

Scattered Pieces of Spring Silkworms

Doubts Caused By

— Yan Bai Bi

丨Are Actors Who Are Suitable for Urban Themes Also Suitable for Rural Themes?丨

Mao Dun's "Spring Silkworms" is a work that exposes the collapse of rural areas.

I think the causes of "Spring Silkworms" are nothing more than: the original author grew up in the countryside and experienced the real sense of the collapse of rural areas, analyzed and investigated with rich social science knowledge, and wrote with active new literary techniques.

This "Spring Silkworms" is of course a valuable harvest in literature and art. Now, it has been selected as a theme by the Star Film Company, and director Cheng Bugao has started filming it. It will be more truly unfolded in front of a wider audience. I can't help but congratulate the word deeply.

But recently, from the star monthly magazine of the Star Film Company, I saw a few scattered pieces of "Spring Silkworms" that they had already filmed, but I instinctively felt that what "Spring Silkworms" described was not the collapsed rural area, but the urbanized rural area! Although this is a small matter about the background, the "unreal" of the small matter will also affect the overall effect. Therefore, I am worried about the guidance and actors of the entire film industry. Are directors and actors who are suitable for urban themes also suitable for rural themes? Are directors and actors who are used to urban life and have no real sense of rural collapse suitable for filming films with rural themes? Editor's note: This is a letter of opinion. I am now publishing it with an impartial attitude, and I hope to arouse the attention of relevant parties. Not Sensitive

All Star Cast

In the past year or two, the European and American film industries have been extremely embarrassed due to the impact of the world's economic depression. In order to recover the declining business situation, they had to use All Star Cast to attract the audience. Of course, whether this type of film can achieve good results is a question, but in the substance of the film, it did improve the level of performance

The sound blockbuster "Two Against One" (directed by Zhang Shichuan) that the Star Film Company is currently filming can also be said to be China's first All Star Cast film. Because in addition to Hu Die, almost all the stars of the Star Film Company are included. A new level of performance will be presented to us in the near future.

Tour of European and American Photography Fields (8)

— Yun Yan

(10) Islington (UK) Islington

丨Gainsborough Film Company's film studio in Islington, London丨 Leaving the bustling streets of London, in that area of factories, warehouses and shacks, before the European War, there was a power plant that supplied the city's railway current. The chimney of that power plant still stands; but the buildings below have now become the Gainsborough Film Company's film studio.

The American Lask Film Company purchased the land in 1919 and built a photography studio. In the next four years, Islington Photography Studio became the birthplace of excellent films. In 1923, they specialized in renting this film studio to other companies to make films. Phyllis Konstam, was then one of the outstanding stars of Islington. The following year, three adventurous London businessmen 丨Friedman, Saville and Balcon 丨 formed a new company and rented here to make films. Not long after, the Gainsborough Company was established, and this place became its property. By 1927. and installed radios to shoot sound films. In 1930. Unfortunately, the god of fire came and burned the tops of the two theaters to a crisp. In the spring of 1931, the reconstructed new-style film studio was completed. Although the design has been changed, the equipment on the second floor remains the same as the old style. The area of Theater No. 1 on the bottom floor is 6,264 square feet, and the theater on the upper floor is 5,244 square feet. The top floor is a platform, which is prepared for shooting outside, and there are three projection rooms inside; one is on the bottom floor, almost as large as an ordinary small theater, and there are two smaller ones underground.

(11) Shepherd's Bush (UK) Shepherds Bush

丨Gaumont Film Company's film studio in Shepherd's Bush, West London丨

Gaumont in England is the same as Paramount in Hollywood. Hollywood's first film studio was in a farmhouse in a forest, and the result was the production of Paramount's large film studio. And Gaumont, in 1898, was only filming films in the Durvich Civic Cricket Ground. But now they already own the best film studio in England. (To be continued)
